  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stick butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onion</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; elbow macaroni&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced, cooked chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 15-oz.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans tomato sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 cans&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span> <span class="T8">- or more</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Sauté onion in butter in very large skillet. &nbsp;Mix dry macaroni in butter and onion till coated and yellowed. &nbsp;Add tomato sauce and water and seasonings. &nbsp;Cover and simmer 15 minutes, stirring occasionally. &nbsp;Add water if needed.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add chicken that has been pulled apart. &nbsp;Cook 5 minutes more. &nbsp;Cover with grated cheese and simmer until cheese melts.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serves 14-16. &nbsp;This is tripled from the original recipe.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P31"><span class="T15">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Chicken Strata</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">12-15&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; slices day-old bread&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onions</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dash&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cheddar cheese, grated</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced, cooked chicken&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped celery</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 cans&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream of mushroom soup</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">salt to taste&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh sliced mushrooms&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen green peas</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Reserving 5 slices for later, cut remaining bread into 1" cubes. &nbsp;Place half in bottom of greased 15x10 pan.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook celery, mushrooms, &amp; onions in 1 tbl butter. &nbsp;Combine chicken, vegetables, mayonnaise, and seasonings. &nbsp;Spoon over bread cubes. &nbsp;Sprinkle remaining cubes over chicken mixture. &nbsp;Combine eggs and milk; pour over all. &nbsp;Cover and chill at least 1 hour or over night.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp;Preheat oven to 350º. &nbsp;Butter the five reserved slices of bread. &nbsp;Cut into ½" cubes. Spoon soups over top and sprinkle with buttered cubes of bread. &nbsp;Bake at 350º for 1 hour. &nbsp;Sprinkle cheese on top last few minutes of cooking. &nbsp;Serves 10-12. &nbsp;This recipe has been enlarged from the original.</span></p>
  <p class="P11">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P11">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T3">Southwest White Chili</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 ½ &nbsp;lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cooked chicken, diced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 4-oz.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans chopped green chilies</span> <span class="T8">-mild</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cilantro</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans white beans, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tbl.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lime juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Heat oil in 2 to 3-qt saucepan. &nbsp;Add chicken cubes and cook 4-5 minutes. &nbsp;Remove with slotted spoon and keep warm. &nbsp;Add onion to saucepan and cook 2 minutes. &nbsp;Stir in broth, green chilies and all the spices. &nbsp;Simmer 30 minutes. &nbsp;Stir in cooked chicken, lime juice and beans. &nbsp;Simmer 10 minutes. &nbsp;Garnish with Monterey Jack cheese and onions, if desired. Makes 4 servings. My kids liked this served with hot, buttered sourdough bread!</span></p>

  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Chicken Lickin'</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless, skinless chicken breasts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; clove garlic&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">4 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced mushrooms, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; heavy cream</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Slice chicken and place in crockpot. &nbsp;Add all ingredients except cream. &nbsp;Cook on LOW 6-8 hours. &nbsp;Add cream just before serving. &nbsp;Serve over spaghetti noodles or chicken-flavored couscous. &nbsp;Serves 6-8 with lots of sauce!</span></p>

  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Chicken Tetrazzini</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thin spaghetti&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">10 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can cream mushroom soup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">4 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced black olives, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">4 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced water chestnuts, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced, cooked chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sherry&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced mushrooms, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P27"><span class="T19">Do not add</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Parmesan cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry breadcrumbs</span></p>
  <h1 class="P52"><a id="a__To_freezer_bag"><span></span></a><span class="T21">To freezer bag</span></h1>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook spaghetti; drain. &nbsp;Sauté &nbsp;onions until tender. &nbsp;Combine all ingredients except Parmesan, mixing well. &nbsp;Place in baking dish and top with Parmesan cheese and/or dry breadcrumbs. &nbsp;Bake for 30 minutes at 350º. &nbsp;Serves 8 to 10. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T22">Entire dish can be combined, bagged and frozen, for serving later. &nbsp;Increase baking time if not thawed entirely.</span></p>

  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Chicken Stroganoff</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; From Taste of Home, website</span></p>
  <p class="P53">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 slices&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bacon, diced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless chicken meat</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 med&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onions&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 16 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mushrooms, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 cloves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper to taste&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook bacon until crisp. Drain, reserving 4 tbl drippings; set bacon aside. In drippings, cook chicken, onions, &amp; mushrooms. &nbsp;Add broth, garlic, salt, pepper, paprika, and bacon. &nbsp;Cover &amp; simmer 10 minutes. &nbsp;Combine flour and sour cream until smooth. &nbsp;Add to chicken mixture. &nbsp;Bring to a boil; cook &amp; stir for 2 minutes or until thickened. &nbsp;Serve over noodles. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">This recipe has been doubled from the original.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Oriental Grilled Chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soy sauce (tamari - wheat free)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; roasted peanut oil</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground mustard</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced garlic&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; honey</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless, skinless chicken breasts</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Add all ingredients together in large Ziploc. &nbsp;Shake and mix well. &nbsp;Chill for 3-4 hours. Grill 6 minutes per side on hot grill. &nbsp;Serve with extra soy sauce.</span></p>

  <p class="P67"><span class="T1">Rock Cornish Hens</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Cornish game hens&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; white wine</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves minced garlic&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic salt</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">¾ c &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tarragon</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt and pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Day before</span><span class="T6">:&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Thaw hens and keep refrigerated.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Early in day</span><span class="T6">:&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; In saucepan, combine oil, wine, and 1 tbl tarragon.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In each hen place garlic glove (or powder), 1 tsp. tarragon, ¼ tsp. salt, 1/8 tsp. pepper. &nbsp;Sprinkle outside liberally with garlic salt. &nbsp;Refrigerate.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large shallow pan without rack, roast hens 1 hour or until well browned and drumstick twists easily out of thigh. &nbsp;Baste often with wine sauce.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serve with wild rice. &nbsp;Serves 4.</span></p>

  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Peanut Butter Chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T4"><br></span><span class="T6">4-6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Boneless, skinless chicken breasts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 clove&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coriander</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1/4c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soy sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 Tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">3 Tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peanut butter</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder</span></p>
  <p class="P4">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp;Combine all the ingredients together (I usually use a zip lock baggie) and let marinate in the refrigerator at least 2 hours.&nbsp; I usually fix this in the morning.&nbsp; Remove from the marinade and broil or barbecue until slightly brown and the meat is no longer pink when slashed, about 5-6 minutes on a side. DO NOT OVER COOK! &nbsp; Double recipe for up to 12 breasts.<br></span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Potato Shake&nbsp;-n-Bake for Chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Place in gallon ziploc bag and shake to mix:</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; instant mashed potato flakes</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tsp to 1 tbl garlic powder (depends on how garlicky you like it!)</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Into a small bowl, pour equal parts plain yogurt and your favorite&nbsp;salad dressing (creamy or oil-based, whatever!)</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Coat each chicken piece in dressing mix and then drop into bag of flakes.&nbsp; Shake bag to coat.&nbsp; Remove chicken and&nbsp;lay on Pam-sprayed cookie sheet.&nbsp; Repeat for all chicken pieces.&nbsp; I often have to stop and make a little more flake mixture - depending on how much chicken I'm cooking.</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Place chicken in oven at 350.&nbsp; If boneless, check in 15 minutes.&nbsp; DON'T TURN.&nbsp;&nbsp;As soon as it isn't pink, it's done.&nbsp; Don't&nbsp;over cook - it will get dry.&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P28"><span class="T3">Deep-Dish Chicken Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">2½-3 lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stalks celery, cut up</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; small onion, quartered&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaf</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; margarine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced fresh mushrooms</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large leek or onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced celery</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red bell pepper, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; poultry seasoning&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P40"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; light cream or milk</span></p>
  <p class="P19"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen peas&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg, beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P20"><span class="T6">1 of 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; refrigerated, folded, unbaked piecrusts</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Rinse chicken. &nbsp;Place in large stockpot; add 5 cups water. &nbsp;Add celery, onion, bay leaf, 1 tsp. salt, and ¼ tsp. pepper. &nbsp;Bring to boil; reduce heat. &nbsp;Cover and simmer for 45 to 60 minutes. &nbsp;Remove chicken and set aside. &nbsp;Strain broth. &nbsp;Discard vegetables and bay leaf. &nbsp;Pull chicken meat from bones and cut meat into ½" cubes. &nbsp;Discard bones and skin.</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large saucepan melt margarine over medium heat. &nbsp;Add mushrooms, leeks, sliced celery, and red pepper. &nbsp;Cook about 3 minutes or till tender. &nbsp;Stir in flour, poultry seasoning, ½ tsp. salt, and ¼ tsp. pepper. &nbsp;Add 1½ c broth and cream all at once; cook and stir till thickened and bubbly. &nbsp;Stir in chicken and peas; pour into a round 1½ qt casserole dish</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Unfold piecrust. &nbsp;Cut into circle 2" larger in diameter than top of dish. &nbsp;Brushed edge of dish with egg. &nbsp;Place crust atop casserole; turn edge under and flute to top edge of dish. &nbsp;Cut a 1" hole in center of crust for steam to escape. &nbsp;Cut pastry scraps into decorative strips; brush top of crust with egg and lay on strips. &nbsp;Brush again with egg. &nbsp;Bake at 400º for 30 to 40 minutes or till crust is golden brown. &nbsp;Serve immediately. &nbsp;Makes 6 servings.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">&nbsp;Chicken Wild Rice Salad</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">3 boxes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Uncle Ben's Wild Rice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 cans&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced water chestnuts, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced, cooked chicken&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">4 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; seedless grapes, cut in halves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cashews</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ &nbsp;tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Cook rice according to pkg directions. &nbsp;Let cool to room temperature. &nbsp;Add remaining ingredients, except for cashews, and chill. &nbsp;Serve with cashews as topping - don't add into salad as they become soggy in leftover salad. &nbsp;Serves 10-12.</span></p>

  <p class="Title">Artichoke Chicken</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From Taste of Home, J/A 2002</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2-14oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans water-packed artichoke hearts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Parmesan cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">8&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless, skinless chicken breasts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Drain artichokes well and chop. &nbsp;In a bowl, combine all ingredients except chicken. &nbsp;Place chicken on greased 15x10 jelly roll pan, spaced slightly apart. &nbsp;Spread artichoke mixture on top of each chicken breast - it will not spread as it cooks. &nbsp;Bake, uncovered, at 375 for 35 minutes, or until chicken juices run clear and tops are golden brown. &nbsp;Serve over buttered noodles.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">NOTE: &nbsp;This recipe has been doubled from the original which called for 4 chicken breasts cooked in a 13x9 pan. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Chicken with Paprika Cream</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From Taste of Home, F/M 2004</span></p>
  <p class="P53">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless, skinless chicken breasts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, divided</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onions, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1-2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; heavy whipping cream</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">In large skillet, brown chicken in 1 tablespoon of butter and oil. &nbsp;Cover and cook 5-7 minutes or until juices run clear. &nbsp;Remove chicken; keep warm.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">In same skillet, sauté onions until tender. Reduce heat to medium. Add paprika and remaining butter; heat until butter is melted. Stir in cream, salt and pepper; cook and wstir until sauce is thickened, about 4 minutes. Serve with chicken over rice. &nbsp;Garnish with additional green onions, if desired. &nbsp;Serves 6. &nbsp;Recipe can easily be doubled.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Creamed Chicken and Biscuits</span></p>
  <p class="P56">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless, skinless chicken breasts - cooked &amp; cut into small pieces</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream of chicken soup</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whole milk</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped pimiento&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1-2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese, divided</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tarragon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">4oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can mushrooms, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 12&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen biscuits, thawed</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. Grease 13x9 pan. &nbsp;Saute onion in butter until tender. &nbsp;Combine onion, chicken, soup, sour cream, milk, and pimiento in a medieum bowl and mix well. &nbsp;Spoon mixture into baking dish. &nbsp;Bake 20 minutes. &nbsp;Remove from oven. &nbsp;Sprinkle baked layer with half of grated cheddar. &nbsp;Arrange biscuits in single layer over top. &nbsp;Sprinkle with remaining cheddar cheese. &nbsp;Make until biscuits are golden brown and the sauce is bubbly, ablut 25-30 minutes longer. &nbsp;Serve immediately.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Amish Chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P56">&nbsp;</p>
  <ol>
    <li>
      <p class="P1" style="margin-left:0cm;"><span style="display:block;float:left;min-width:1.27cm;">2</span><span class="T6">whole chickens (about 4 lbs each)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coarse salt</span><span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; black pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery powder</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 200. Rinse chickens and pat dry. Combine spices and rub over and inside both chickens. &nbsp;Place chickens in large roasting pan breast side down. &nbsp;Cover tightly and bake for about 8 hours. &nbsp;For ornery old roosters, cook 12 hours or so. &nbsp;Use kitchen shears to cut legs &amp; wings off, the rest will fall off the bones!</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Chicken Wraps</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cooked chicken meat, deboned</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Lettuce, tomatos, black olive slices</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Olive Garden salad dressing</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">On cookie sheet, place tortilla lightly covered in grated cheese. &nbsp;In center strip, add chicken, and black olives. Bake at 350 for 5 minutes or until cheese has just begun to melt. &nbsp;Don't let tortillas get crispy! &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P37"><span class="T2">&nbsp;</span><span class="T5">Ann Landers' Meatloaf</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1 lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cracker crumbs</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">½ lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground veal&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ketchup</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground pork&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; warm water</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 pkg.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry onion soup mix</span></p>
  <ol>
    <li>
      <p class="P44" style="margin-left:3.6619cm;"><span style="display:block;float:left;min-width:1.1219cm;">2</span><span class="T6">eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span> <span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="P27_borderStart"><span class="T19">do not add</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8-oz.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can tomato sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P27_borderEnd"><span class="T19">to freezer bag</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; strips bacon</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350º. &nbsp;Mix meats together by hand in large bowl. &nbsp;Add Worcestershire, eggs, cracker crumbs, ketchup, water, and soup mix. &nbsp;Mix. &nbsp;Shape into a loaf in a shallow baking dish. &nbsp;Drape loaf with bacon strips and then pour tomato sauce over loaf. &nbsp;Bake 1½ to 2 hours, or until done to your liking.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients, except in box, in freezer bag; shape correctly, freeze and cook later.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serves 6 to 8.</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green bell pepper, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ketchup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can tomato sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vinegar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar</span></p>

Add remaining ingredients. &nbsp;Simmer15 minutes (or longer - won't matter). &nbsp;Serve on hamburger buns. &nbsp;Serves 4 to 5. &nbsp;</span> <span class="T22">May be frozen in bags and served later.</span></p>

  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Meatballs in Tomato Stroganoff</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P21"><span class="T6">½ lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1clove&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P21"><span class="T6">¼ lb. each&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground pork and veal&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry breadcrumbs</span></p>
  <p class="P21"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp. &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P21">1<span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;egg</span><span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp; ½ tsp. ea. thyme, black pepper</span> <span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P72_borderStart"><span class="T8">Do not add</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6oz can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato paste</span></p>
  <p class="P72_borderEnd"><span class="T8">to freezer bag</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dill</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine meats, garlic, breadcrumbs, milk, eggs, salt, pepper, and thyme. &nbsp;Make into small balls (approx. 16 one-inch balls.) &nbsp;Brown meatballs.</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P45"><span class="T22">Recipe can be frozen at this point. &nbsp;Bag up meatballs and freeze.</span></p>
  <p class="P17">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine meatballs, broth, dill, and tomato paste. &nbsp;Cover and simmer 15 minutes. &nbsp;Add in sour cream, stir till smooth. &nbsp;Serve over egg noodles, rice or mashed potatoes. &nbsp;Recipe is easily doubled or quadrupled. &nbsp;Made with all beef tastes good, too! &nbsp;I add finely minced onion and sliced mushrooms to tomato sauce. &nbsp;My kids beg for this dinner!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Bulk Cooking Meatballs</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ½ &nbsp;lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef, pork or combination&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 &nbsp;c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry breadcrumbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¼ tsp ea. Thyme, black pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Heat oven to 375. &nbsp;Cover all baking sheets with foil and then parchment paper. &nbsp;This will make clean up easier without food touching aluminum. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix all ingredients very well &nbsp;in Bosch mixer with dough hook. &nbsp;With cookie scoop, scoop the mixture and place in rows on pans close together. &nbsp;Bake for 20-30 minutes. &nbsp;They should be lightly browned, not overcooked, and not pink in the center. &nbsp;Cool and place in freezer bags. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">NOTE: &nbsp;Any meatball recipe will work with this cooking method -</span> <span class="T17">just don't add more than 2 ½ lbs of meat to the mixer per batch</span><span class="T6">. &nbsp;I usually do 5 lbs of meat at a time in two batches - makes 4 freezer bags worth of meals.</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Inside Out Grape Leaves</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic clove, crushed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 28oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10oz pkgs frozen chopped spinach&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uncooked rice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dill weed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ &nbsp;tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In an 8qt stock pot, cook beef, onion, and garlic over med-high heat, stirring often, until beef is crumbly and browned. &nbsp;Drain off excess fat. &nbsp;Thaw spinach, &nbsp;but do not drain.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Stir in tomatoes (with juice), spinach, rice, dill weed, salt and pepper. &nbsp;Heat to a simmer, then reduce heat to low. &nbsp;Cover and simmer 30-40 minutes, or until rice is tender. &nbsp;Add small amounts of water as it cooks, if it starts to stick.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Pressure Cooker Beef Stew</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lean stew meat&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; seasoned flour (Margo Brooks's recipe)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, peeled and sliced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; potatoes, cubed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh mushrooms, quartered</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced garlic&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Kimball garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef boullion cubes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; good red wine</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 15-oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Heat oil in pressure cooker. &nbsp;Coat stew meat pieces with seasoned flour, reserving leftover flour. &nbsp;Brown pieces in batches, drain on paper towels. &nbsp;Add vegetables and tomatoes, bring burner up to high. &nbsp;Add remaining ingredients and return meat to pot. &nbsp;Stir bottom well to loosen brown bits. &nbsp;Bring to a boil, put on lid, and bring cooker to 2</span><span class="T25">nd</span> <span class="T6">red ring. &nbsp;Reduce burner to 2 ½ and then set timer to 20 minutes. &nbsp;When timer goes off, turn of burner but leave pot in place 30 minutes without opening. &nbsp;Then open, add remaining flour which has been mix with a small amount of cold water until lump-free. &nbsp;Bring back to a simmer to thicken. &nbsp;Add salt to taste. &nbsp;Serve over egg noodles. &nbsp;Serves 12.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Creamy Ham &amp; Macaroni</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T26">From Taste of Home, D/J 2005, pg 31</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uncooked macaroni&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, cubed</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken bouillon granules&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shredded cheddar, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cubed fully cooked ham</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated Parmesan cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook macaroni, drain and set aside. &nbsp;In 6-qt stockpot, melt butter and whisk in flour until smooth. &nbsp;Whisk in the milk, bouillon and pepper. &nbsp;Bring to a boil; cook and stir for 2 minutes or until thickened. &nbsp;Remove from the heat. &nbsp;Stir in 2 cups of cheddar cheese, ham, Parmesan and macaroni. &nbsp;Transfer to greased 13x9 pan. Sprinkle with remaining cheddar cheese. &nbsp;Bake, uncovered at 350 for 20-25 minutes or until bubbly. &nbsp;Serves 12. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">This recipe has been doubled from the original.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Salisbury Steak</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Taste of Home, D/J '06, pg 56</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry bread crumbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown gravy mix</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried minced onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lean ground beef</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a bowl, whisk the eggs and milk. &nbsp;Add bread crumbs, gravy mix and onion. &nbsp;Crumble beef over mixture and mix well. &nbsp;Shape into 12 patties about ¾" thick. &nbsp;Spray broiler pan with Pam and cover with patties. &nbsp;Broil 3-4 inches (2</span><span class="T25">nd</span> <span class="T6">rack position from the top) for 6-7 minutes on each side. &nbsp;Serve with lots of Salisbury Gravy and mashed potatoes! &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">For gravy, mix up brown gravy mix according to directions for making 2 cups of gravy. &nbsp;Add 4 tbl of prepared yellow mustard to gravy and whisk thoroughly until well blended. &nbsp;Heat until thickened. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Pepper Steak &amp; Rice</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Grandma Norris</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tenderized round steak&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 cloves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, crushed</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced green onions</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green peppers, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornstarch</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soy sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh mushrooms, sliced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large fresh tomatoes, cut into eighths</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cut meat into ¼" wide strips; sprinkle with paprika and set aside 5 minutes. &nbsp;Brown meat in butter. &nbsp;Add garlic and broth. &nbsp;Cover and simmer 30 minutes. &nbsp;Stir in onions, mushrooms, and green peppers. Cover and cook 5 minutes. &nbsp;Blend cornstarch, water and soy sauce until smooth. &nbsp;Stir into meat mixture. &nbsp;Cook stirring until clear and thickened. &nbsp;Add tomatoes and stir gently. &nbsp;Serve over rice.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">BBQ Burgers</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5-6 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef or pork roast(s)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; BBQ Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Hamburger buns&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Place meat in crockpot. &nbsp;Season with:</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Salt &amp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Onion powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Chili powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Paprika&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Liquid smoke</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Do not add any other liquid. &nbsp;Cook about 7 hours on high. &nbsp;Remove meat from crockpot. Shred meat, removing fat &amp; bones. &nbsp;Place in serving dish with a lid, pouring 1 cup defatted juice from crockpot over shredded meat.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Pour 1 ½ c BBQ sauce of your choice over meat. &nbsp;Stir. &nbsp;Keep warm in oven until serving time. &nbsp;Serve with additional BBQ sauce.</span></p>
