  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cincinnati Skyline Chili</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 qt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">32 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground allspice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 7 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground cloves</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; medium onion, finely chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add ground beef to water in 8 qt stockpot. &nbsp;Do not turn on heat yet! &nbsp;Use plunger blender to puree to fine texture. &nbsp;Boil slowly for 30 minutes. &nbsp;Add all other ingredients, bring to a boil. &nbsp;Reduce heat and simmer uncovered for 3 hours. &nbsp;Pot may be covered the last hour after desired consistency reached. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Chili should be served with &nbsp;hot spaghetti noodles, red kidney beans, finely diced onions, lots of cheddar cheese, saltine crackers, and vinegar pepper sauce. &nbsp;Makes approx 1 gallon of chili.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Sausage Potato Bake</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cubed &nbsp;potatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; kielbasa sausage, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large onions</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh mushrooms</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bell pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper &amp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 425. &nbsp;Mix potatoes, oil, salt, pepper, and garlic powder. &nbsp;Divide potatoes onto 3 greased jelly roll pans. &nbsp;Stir occasionally to brown evenly.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Chop remaining vegetables &amp; sausage. &nbsp;Add them to the pans when you remove them to stir. &nbsp;Add carrots earlier than mushrooms, onions, or sausage as they take longer to cook. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Optional: &nbsp;When potatoes are done, serve with a few fried eggs on top or to the side.</span></p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Homemade Beef Salami</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; liquid smoke</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mustard seeds</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coarsely ground pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion powder</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; crushed red pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef (80% lean or leaner)</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">5 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Morton's Tender Quick</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine water, liquid smoke, spices and Tender Quick. &nbsp;Add beef and knead with hands, mixing well. &nbsp;Divide meat into 3 rolls. &nbsp;Wrap each roll separately in heavy-duty foil. &nbsp;Meat will be soft and moist, so be sure to use heavy-duty foil. Wrap foil tightly closed down center and seal ends. &nbsp;Refrigerate for at least 24 hours.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Using a fork, make holes through the foil on the bottom of each roll, about 1 inch apart. &nbsp;Place rolls on the rack of a broiler pan with the hole pierced part on the underneath. &nbsp;Place hot water in the shallow pan of the broiler, underneath the rack. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Bake in center of oven at 325 for 2 hours. &nbsp;Remove foil and set rolls on rack to drain and cool. &nbsp;Slice as desired. &nbsp;Cover and store in refrigerator for up to ten days, or freeze.</span></p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Meat and Beans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3-4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried pinto beans&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boiling water</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can tomato sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can mild Rotel tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 pc&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt pork&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; clove garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Great in 6-qt crockpot! Soak rinsed, sorted beans in salted water overnight. Drain and rinse well. Turn crockpot to HIGH. &nbsp;Pour boiling water into crockpot, until beans are covered with about 1 inch of water. &nbsp;Add the piece of salt pork and let cook. &nbsp;Check after a few hours for enough water. &nbsp;Beans should be cooked in about 3 hours.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook onions and ground meat; drain. &nbsp;Remove salt pork and separate meat from fat and return meat to crockpot along with ground meat, onions, and remaining ingredients. &nbsp;Turn crockpot down to LOW and let simmer 4 more hours.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serve with sour cream or plain yogurt, salsa, or chopped green onions. &nbsp;We enjoy it with Chipotle Tabasco sauce or other hot sauces. &nbsp;Corn bread and salad completes the meal! &nbsp;Serves 10-12 or freeze half for later. &nbsp;Becomes thicker when cooled and reheated. &nbsp;Makes great leftovers (serve over rice to extend)!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P11">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T3">Saucy Beef Strips</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 ½ lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; round steak or stew meat&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; clove garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green bell pepper, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrot, shredded&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 16 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canned diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef bouillon cube&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn starch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Slice beef into strips and place in crockpot. &nbsp;Add remaining ingredients, except cornstarch. &nbsp;Cook on HIGH 6-8 hours. &nbsp;Thicken with cornstarch before serving. &nbsp;Serve over noodles or rice, topped with lots of grated cheddar cheese. &nbsp;Kids liked this one! &nbsp;Serves 4.</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Saenz Stroganoff</span></p>
  <p class="P3"></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef bouillon cubes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 bottles beer</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">1 ½ lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cubed beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Basil</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Thyme&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Marjoram</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Salt</span></p>
  <p class="P9"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; All purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Great recipe for the crockpot! &nbsp;Place all ingredients except flour and sour cream in crockpot. &nbsp;Stir so that all meat pieces are coated and covered. &nbsp;Cover and cook on low setting for 4 hours.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 HOURS before serving time: Remove 2c cooking liquid. &nbsp;Mix in flour to hot liquid. &nbsp;Stir until smooth. &nbsp;Pour back into crockpot. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 HOUR before serving time: Add in sour cream. &nbsp;Stir until sour cream is well mixed into sauce.</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T22">Beer can be replaced with water, but beer gives it a better flavor. &nbsp;Plain yogurt or 'light-sour cream' both work well here. &nbsp;Be sure to mix well! &nbsp;I always add sliced mushrooms and chopped onions.</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Grandma Saenz brought this recipe back from Europe, during their years stationed there. &nbsp;It is traditionally served over made-from-scratch French fries! &nbsp;Delicious!!! &nbsp;(Oven baked &nbsp;works well at our house!) &nbsp;Can also be served over noodles or rice.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Pakistani Beef and Peas</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic clove, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1-1½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; curry powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">14oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canned diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; each salt and pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced fresh ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen peas</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Brown beef in 4-qt Dutch oven with onions. &nbsp;Add tomatoes with juice, ginger, garlic, curry powder, salt and pepper. &nbsp;Cook, stirring 1 minute.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Stir in ½ c water and lemon juice and bring to a boil. &nbsp;Reduce heat to medium-low and simmer until liquid is evaporated, about 15 minutes. &nbsp;Stir in peas during last few minutes of cooking to heat through. &nbsp;Serve over rice.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Other veggies can be added: broccoli spears, chopped green beans, or diced boiled potato.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Lamb Meatball Stew with Barley</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground lamb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1-2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried mint</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lecithin granules,optional</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">14oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; white kidney beans, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 28oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes, undrained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large carrot, peeled &amp; diced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced fresh mushrooms</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery ribs, diced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pearl barley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; juice &amp; peel of one lemon</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In 6 qt dutch oven, combine lamb, mint, flour, lecithin, egg, garlic salt and pepper. &nbsp;Using your hands, mix ingredients together well. &nbsp;Form into 1 ½ " meatballs and set aside on wax paper.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In same pan, combine broth, beans, tomatoes with their liquid, carrots, mushrooms, celery, and barley. &nbsp;Stir to mix. &nbsp;Heat to boiling; reduce heat to low. &nbsp;CAREFULLY add meatballs. &nbsp;Cover and simmer 1 ½ hrs. &nbsp;Stir very gently. &nbsp;Stir in lemon peel and juice. &nbsp;Add salt to taste. &nbsp;Sprinkle with parsley and serve.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Herbed Lamb</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; leg of lamb, about 6 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onions, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4-5&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves of garlic&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; claret wine or dry red wine</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cut deep slits in lamb, about 2 inches apart, over entire surface. Crush garlic; mix with salt, oregano, and pepper. Press mixture evenly into all slits in meat. Place meat on rack in pan with fat side up. Do not cover. Roast at 325 for 30-35 minutes per pound for medium. If using a meat thermometer, roast meat to 175 for medium or 180 for well done. Combine wine, green onions, and lemon juice; reserve ½ of this basting mixture for the gravy. Baste lamb often with remaining half of mixture. When meat is done, put on warm platter, skim fat off juices, reserving 1 cup. &nbsp;Melt butter and blend in flour. Stir in reserved wine mixture and meat juices. &nbsp;Cook and stir until thickened. Serve sauce separately.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">NOTE</span><span class="T6">: &nbsp;Took 1 hr, 55 minutes for medium roast that weighed 3.89 lbs, cooked at 325.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Good Shepherd's Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground turkey or beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 med&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato paste</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; basil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaf</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh mushrooms, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen green beans</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">(8 servings of prepared mashed potatoes)</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients to browned turkey. &nbsp;Make mashed potatoes for 8 servings (about 2 lbs, cooked &amp; mashed). &nbsp;Place meat sauce into a 13x9 pan. &nbsp;Place potatoes on top (pipe with ziploc bag, if desired). &nbsp;Sprinkle with parsley. &nbsp;Bake uncovered for 30 minutes at 350. &nbsp;Serve with grated cheddar cheese.</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Pesto Pork Roast</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From Taste of Home</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pork roast&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 32 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 12 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pesto sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Layer onion slices and then fresh or canned tomatoes in bottom of 13x9 baking dish. &nbsp;Place roast on top and generously salt and pepper it. &nbsp;Evenly coat roast with pesto sauce. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 1 ½ to 2 hours or until meat thermometer reads 160. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serve with egg noodles mixed with the tomato/pesto pan drippings. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Mushroom Pork</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From Quick Cooking M/J 2004</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pork tenderloin or thick-cut pork chops&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; clove garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced fresh mushrooms</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (or 2 4-oz cans mushrooms)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ &nbsp;tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried marjoram&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ &nbsp;c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cold water</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Rub pork on all sides with garlic; sprinkle with paprika. &nbsp;In large skillet, brown the pork in butter. &nbsp;Add mushrooms, lemon juice, marjoram, salt and pepper. &nbsp;Turn meat to coat with seasonings. &nbsp;Cover and simmer 25-30 minutes or until a meat thermometer reads 160 and juices run clear. &nbsp;Remove meat and keep warm.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a small bowl, combine flour and cold water until smooth; stir into the pan juices. &nbsp;Bring to boil; cook and stir for 2 minutes or until thickened. &nbsp;Slice pork if using tenderloin. &nbsp;Serve with gravy over hot &nbsp;rice.</span></p>
  <p class="P12">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P43">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P43">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Brochette of Pork</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Marinade:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soy sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, finely chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; freshly grated ginger</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; honey&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red wine vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Meat:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ½ lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless loin of pork&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil for brushing pork&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coriander, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine marinade ingredients in mixing bowl. &nbsp;Cut pork into 1 ½ inch cubes and put in soy mixture. Cover. Let stand until ready to cook. Preheat grill or broiler. Drain pork, but reserve liquid. Arrange pork cubes on skewers. Brush meat with oil. Place skewers on grill. Cook, brushing with reserved marinade and turning often so meat cooks evenly, about 15 minutes. In small saucepan, combine ¼ c of marinade, lemon juice, butter and coriander. &nbsp;Heat thoroughly. Spoon onto meat and serve hot.</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">THIS MARINADE AND BUTTER SAUCE IS GREAT WITH CHICKEN, BEEF, OR STIR-FRY, TOO!!</span></p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Chinese Stuffed Peppers</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From 365Ways to Cook Hamburger, pg 134</span></p>
  <p class="P7">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med bell peppers&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; long-grain white rice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh minced ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 clove&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef or pork&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen peas, thawed</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soy sauce, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry sherry, divided</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef broth</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 375. &nbsp;Slice peppers in half and remove seeds &amp; membranes. Fill 13x9 pan.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In med saucepan, of boiling salted water, cook rice 7 minutes. Drain, rinse under cold water, drain again. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In med skillet, heat oil. &nbsp;Add scallions, ginger and garlic and cook over med-high heat until softened and fragrant but not browned, about 1 minute. &nbsp;Transfer to medium bowl. &nbsp;Add meat, peas, rice, 2 tbl soy sauce, 1tbl sherry, and ¼ tsp pepper to bowl. &nbsp;Mix gently but thoroughly to avoid crushing peas. &nbsp;Stuff peppers. In a 2 cup glass measure, combine beef broth, remaining 2 tbl sherry, 1 tbl soy sauce, and ¼ tsp pepper. &nbsp;Pour sauce over peppers and cover dish tightly with foil.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Bake 45 minutes. &nbsp;Remove foil from dish, reduce oven to 350, and continue baking 15 more minutes, basting a few times with sauce. &nbsp; Serves 6.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Granny's Swiss Steak</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stalk celery, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cube steaks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can mushrooms, undrained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt, or to taste&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 pkg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry onion soup mix</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper, or to taste&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bell pepper, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can tomato sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Heat oil in large skillet over medium-high heat. &nbsp;Dredge steaks in mixture of flour, salt and pepper, and brown them in the hot oil.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Arrange steaks in a 9x13 baking dish. &nbsp;Sprinkle the bell peppers, onion, celery, mushrooms, oregano and onion soup mix over the steaks. &nbsp;Pour tomato sauce over all. &nbsp;Bake for 1 hour.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P28"><span class="T3">Tuna Patties</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">18 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canned tuna**, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried, seasoned bread crumbs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely diced onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil &amp; margarine</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix all ingredients well in large mixing bowl. &nbsp;Heat oil and butter in large skillet over medium heat. &nbsp;Form patties and place in hot oil. Brown each side, 3-4 minutes. &nbsp;Place on warm serving platter until ready to serve. &nbsp;Makes 12 patties. &nbsp;Recipe works well when doubled, just use very large bowl and a sturdy spoon! &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">** Can also be used with boneless, skinless salmon.</span></p>

  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">He-Man Tuna Noodle Casserole</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">18 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg noodles&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter or margarine</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10oz can &nbsp;cream of mushroom soup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1½ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 small&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; jar diced pimento</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green bell pepper, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; heaping cupfuls &nbsp;tuna, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery, finely chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 30&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Ritz crackers (one stack)</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley for garnish</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook and drain noodles. &nbsp;Sauté onions, celery, and bell peppers until soft. Combine all ingredients, except crackers and parsley. &nbsp;Place in baking dish; top with crushed Ritz crackers and parsley. Bake 30 minutes at 425º. &nbsp;Makes 2 13x9 pans.</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">[Note: &nbsp; Don't add cracker crumbs if freezing first - add only just before cooking.]</span></p>

  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Shrimp, Tomato, and Basil Linguine</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; linguine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 bunch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh broccoli, cut into florets</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red wine vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced red bell pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onions, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water-packed basil, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/8 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cooked, peeled, med to lg shrimp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lime juice</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated Parmesan cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P6">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">In large pot of boiling water, cook pasta and broccoli until just tender; drain well. &nbsp;Transfer to large bowl.</span></p>
  <p class="P6">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">Add all remaining ingredients except cheese and toss. &nbsp;Serve warm, at room temperature, or chilled. &nbsp;Serve with Parmesan cheese to the side. &nbsp;Serves 6</span></p>
  <p class="P28"><span class="T3">&nbsp;Tomato Lemon Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; extra virgin olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can diced tomatoes, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon peel or zest&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced black olives</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add olive oil, drained tomatoes, lemon peel, juice, parsley, salt and pepper. &nbsp;Heat thoroughly. &nbsp;Serve over hot pasta with Parmesan, salad, and garlic bread.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Entire recipe can be bagged and frozen for cooking and serving later! &nbsp;Makes 2 ½ c of sauce, serving 4.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Ranch Dressing and Dip Mix</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">from "Quick Cooking" Magazine,</span> <span class="T13"></span><span class="T9">July/Aug 2000, p 19</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried minced onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried parsley flakes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Additional ingredients for dressing</span><span class="T6">:&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span> <span class="T16">Additional ingredients for dip</span><span class="T6">:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In blender, combine the first six ingredients. &nbsp;Blend until onion pieces are small. &nbsp;Store in a quart jar in a cool dry place for up to 1 year. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T15">To prepare dressing:</span> <span class="T6">&nbsp;In a bowl, combine 1 tbl mix with mayo and sour cream; refrigerate. Yield: 2 cups.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T15">To prepare dip:</span> <span class="T6">In a bowl, combine 1 tbl mix and sour cream; refrigerate at least an hour before serving. &nbsp;Yield: 1 cup.</span></p>
  <p class="P54">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P67"><span class="T1">Blender Hollandaise Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T12">from Joy of Cooking, pg 358</span></p>
  <p class="P62">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg yolks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">pinch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cayenne pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, not margarine</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Have ready in your blender everything except the butter. &nbsp;When ready to serve the sauce, melt the butter until it is bubbling and very hot (but not browning).</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cover blender container and turn motor on HIGH. &nbsp;After 3 seconds, remove lid while motor is still going and slowly pour the butter over the eggs in a steady stream. &nbsp;By the time the butter is poured in - about 30 seconds! - the sauce should be finished. &nbsp;If not, blend on HIGH about 5 seconds longer. &nbsp;Serve at once or keep warm by immersing blender container in warm water. &nbsp;This sauce may also be frozen and reconstituted over hot water.</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Seasoned Flour for Frying Chicken</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Margo Brooks</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 ½ - 4c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; marjoram</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; savory</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sage&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Shake all ingredients well. &nbsp;Transfer ½ to bag for shaking chicken and save rest for later use.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cover chicken with flour mixture. &nbsp;Refrigerate 1 hour &amp; reshake &amp; cover chicken again. &nbsp;Fry chicken in ¾" deep oil till golden brown.</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dijon mustard&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 cloves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried Italian seasoning&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground black pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients over pork chops or steaks. &nbsp;Tenderizes; tasted great grilled.</span></p>

  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Taco Seasoning Mix</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried minced onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 &nbsp;tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornstarch</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef boullion powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients and store in a sealed container. &nbsp;Use 2 tbl of mix for each pound of ground beef. &nbsp;After browning and draining meat, add mix and ½ cup water. &nbsp;Simmer till thickened.</span></p>

  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Pesto Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P22">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; packed fresh basil leaves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; freshly grated Parmesan cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; toasted pine nuts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 9 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large garlic cloves</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Process all ingredients except oil in food processor 2 minutes or until smooth, stopping to scrape down sides as needed. &nbsp;Gradually pour oil through food chute with processor running, processing until blended. &nbsp;Divide into 1 ½ c containers; freeze for the future. &nbsp;One container will be enough sauce for 2 lbs of noodles, or lots of pesto garlic bread or 8 pesto chicken breasts.</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar, cumin, paprika, garlic powder</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">MAKE DOUBLE BATCH FOR RICE SALAD.</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Italian Salad Dressing</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix together and store in a sealed pint container:</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl granulated onion</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl each: salt, pepper, dry mustard, thyme, basil, oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Using a salad dressing bottle with the markings on it, fill to the vinegar line with red or white wine vinegar. &nbsp;Then fill with water to the water line. &nbsp;Then add 1 tbl of herb mixture. And then add olive oil to the oil line. &nbsp;Shake and serve. &nbsp;Tastes best if allowed to sit awhile.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Olive Garden Salad Dressing</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a blender, combine the following:</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; white vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn syrup</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Parmesan or Asiago cheese, grated&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Italian seasoning&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley flakes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Blend until smooth. &nbsp;Makes 3 cups or so of dressing. &nbsp;Keep refrigerated. &nbsp;If it separates overnight, just shake before using.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp;To make Olive Garden salad: &nbsp;Pour dressing over chilled salad greens; mix greens well. &nbsp;Then top salad with black olives, red onion rings, whole black olives, tomato, pepperocinis, croutons, and grated Parmesan. &nbsp;Serve immediately. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">BBQ Rib Rub</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T26">From Grassfed Gourmet, pg 253</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; black pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coarse salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients in a quart jar; shake to mix. &nbsp;Rub on ribs the night before cooking, or use on roasts in crockpot for BBQ burgers.</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Ketchup</span></p>
  <p class="P57">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">36 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato paste&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; maple syrup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; t tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sea salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cayenne powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; worchestershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whey (from drained plain yogurt)</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix all ingredients well; use stick blender to smooth. &nbsp;Pour into 2 qt jars. &nbsp;Let sit in dark, cool place 3-4 days to let whey work, then move to refrigerator. &nbsp;Will last one month in fridge. &nbsp;Makes 2 qts.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Dry Onion Soup Mix</span></p>
  <p class="P57">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beef bouillon powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried onion</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; savory</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery seed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Place all ingredients in pint jar. &nbsp;Shake to mix well. &nbsp;5 tbl = 1 packet.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Basic Curry Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P57">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med onions, finely chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic, minced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 inch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; piece of fresh ginger, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; turmeric&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coriander&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato paste + 8 tbl water (</span><span class="T27">or leftover spag sauce)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Heat oil in heavy pan then add onion and stir with heat on high. &nbsp;Add ginger and garlic. &nbsp;Turn heat to low. &nbsp;Cook for 15 minutes stirring from time to time making sure nothing browns or burns. &nbsp;Add turmeric, cumin and coriander and cook, still very gently for a further 5 minutes. &nbsp;Add the tomato paste/water mix and &nbsp;water; stir. &nbsp;Cook slowly without burning until consistency of ketchup. &nbsp;Watch out for splattering.</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <ol>

      <p class="P47" style="margin-left:3.81cm;"><span style="display:block;float:left;min-width:1.27cm;">1</span><span class="T6">lg jar diced pimentos, undrained</span><span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large carrots, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; zucchini, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; yellow bell pepper, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; medium pearl barley</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; black pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh mushrooms, sliced thinly&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 small&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, sliced into thin wedges</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil or butter</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Southern-Style Green Beans</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped celery</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic cloves, crushed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In 4-qt pot, cook bacon until crisp. &nbsp;Remove; drain, reserving 4 tbl drippings in pan. &nbsp;Add onion, celery and garlic to pan; cook and stir over medium heart until tender but not browned, about 4 minutes.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Easy Spinach Casserole</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 boxes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped spinach, thawed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 envelope onion soup mix</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry stuffing mix</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ stick&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Squeeze all the liquid from thawed spinach. &nbsp;Combine sour cream and soup mix until well blended. &nbsp;Add spinach. &nbsp;Mix well. &nbsp;Pour into casserole dish. &nbsp;Can be refrigerated at this point and cooked later. When ready to cook, top with stuffing mix and dot with butter. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 30 minutes, or until stuffing begins to brown. &nbsp;EASY to double! &nbsp;When doubling, put into 2.8L round casserole dish but don't double toppings. &nbsp;Great hit!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Creamed Corn</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; heavy cream</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Bisquick or equivalent</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3 lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen sweet corn&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Parmesan</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Great recipe for the crockpot! &nbsp;Doesn't work as well any other way!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wisk together: milk, cream, sugar, salt, Worcestershire, and Bisquick until smooth. &nbsp;Thaw corn under warm, running water; drain. &nbsp;Place in crockpot. &nbsp;Add milk mixture and stir to coat well. &nbsp;Cook in crockpot on HIGH for 3 to 4 hours. It will not look like anything is happening until the very end of the cooking time. &nbsp;Stir occasionally - especially the bottom. &nbsp;Flour may settle and stick, so scrape bottom corners well.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Garnish with cheese and parsley when serving. &nbsp;Makes enough to freeze half and still have enough for a meal! &nbsp;Very rich! &nbsp;YUM! &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grilled Potato Salad</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; russet potatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red onion</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; spray olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; mayonnaise</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red wine vinegar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dijon mustard&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coarse ground garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thinly sliced celery</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat grill. &nbsp;Peel potatoes and chop into 1" cubes - no larger! &nbsp;Slice onion into ¼" slices. &nbsp;Spray olive oil onto both sides of onion slices and grill on medium until tender. &nbsp;Coat potato chunks with olive oil and salt &amp; pepper. &nbsp; Remove onions from grill and begin grilling potatoes. &nbsp;While those cook, chop grilled onions and mix together with remaining ingredients. &nbsp;When potatoes are very tender, remove from grill and mix with onion mixture. &nbsp;Serve warm.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">If not grilling potatoes, boil halved red potatoes 20-25 minutes, or until tender. Drain, cool, and cut into large-ish chunks. &nbsp;Add dressing while potatoes are warm. &nbsp;Mix with remaining ingredients. &nbsp;Serve warm or chilled. &nbsp;May need to add more dressing after it's chilled. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">[Note: &nbsp;For Jerry's feast, 20 lbs potatoes, 5 large onions, dressing portion of the recipe TIMES 8. &nbsp;Served 120 with small amount leftover.]</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely chopped onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar</span></p>

  <p class="P28"><span class="T4">Luby's Macaroni and Cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry elbow macaroni&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boiling water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ cl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 20&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; slices Am. cheese, torn into pieces</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook macaroni and drain. &nbsp;While it cooks, preheat oven to 35o. Mix together: milk, salt, and flour in a large bowl. &nbsp;Add American cheese and half of the boiling water. &nbsp;Stir well. &nbsp;Then, add remaining boiling water. &nbsp;Beat until smooth and creamy. &nbsp;Cheese should melt well this way. &nbsp;Place half of cheddar into large 15x10 pan. &nbsp; Add hot macaroni and cheese sauce. &nbsp;Mix well. &nbsp;Sprinkle with remaining cheddar. &nbsp;Top with seasoned breadcrumbs, if desired. &nbsp; Bake for 20-30 minutes or until cheese is just beginning to brown on top. 16 servings.</span></p>
  <p class="P23"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cherry Tomato Salad</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Crockpot Dressing</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">12 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry cornbread &amp; bread cubes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, diced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery stalks, sliced thin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stick butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; marjoram&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, well beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Sauté onions and celery in melted butter. &nbsp;Add in parsley and cook until onion is tender. &nbsp;Spray crockpot with Pam. &nbsp;In a large bowl, combine bread cubes, sautéed vegetables, eggs, seasonings, and broth. &nbsp;Once it is well mixed, pour into crockpot. &nbsp;Do not pack it down. &nbsp;Cook on high for 45 minutes, then on low for 4-6 hours. &nbsp;Stir occasionally, as sides will begin browning.</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Mama's Peas</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen green peas&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, sliced in crescents</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4-5&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh mushrooms, sliced thin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a large saucepan, combine water, butter, onions, and mushrooms. &nbsp;Cook over medium high heat until mushrooms are cooked and onions are tender. &nbsp;Add frozen peas and cook until just heated through - not too long.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Macaroni and Tomato Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; macaroni or salad pasta&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2-15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans tomato sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk or cream</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook macaroni until tender and drain well. &nbsp;While draining, melt butter in the same pan over medium heat. &nbsp;Return pasta to pan and stir to coat with butter. &nbsp;Add large can of tomato sauce. &nbsp;Pour milk into tomato sauce can and stir it around and then pour milk onto pasta. &nbsp;Stir well. &nbsp; Season with salt to taste. &nbsp;Reheat leftovers by adding a small amount of milk and stirring while heating.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Bubble and Squeak</span></p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T12">from The Colonial Williamsburg Tavern Cookbook, pg 69</span></p>
  <p class="P63">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4-5&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large potatoes (4lbs)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil, divided</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; medium head green cabbage&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large egg, lightly beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped green onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook peeled potatoes until tender. &nbsp;Drain well and puree. &nbsp;Transfer to a large bowl.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a large skillet, heat half the oil. &nbsp;Add thinly sliced cabbage and season with salt &amp; pepper. &nbsp;Cook over med-high heat, stirring often, until cabbage is tender. &nbsp;Cool slightly.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add cabbage, egg, green onions, and salt &amp; pepper to the potatoes. &nbsp;Mix well to blend and divide into golf-ball size portions. &nbsp;This is much easier with wet hands!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a large skillet over med-high heat, heat remaining oil. &nbsp;Add balls and cook, turning to cook on all sides, until golden brown. &nbsp;Drain on paper towels. &nbsp;Serve with "Blender Hollandaise Sauce" on the top.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Lemon Couscous</span></p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T10">From Southern Living, Oct 2002</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">10 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; couscous&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon rind&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter or margarine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomato</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine broth, lemon rind and juice, and butter in a medium saucepan. &nbsp;Bring to a boil; stir in couscous; cover, remove from heat and let stand 10 minutes. &nbsp;Stir in parsley and tomato.</span></p>

  <p class="P70">Cheesy Hashbrowns</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T14">From Jamie Hays</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; potatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ stick&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, melted&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream of chicken soup</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; crushed cornflakes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cut potatoes into small cubes; boil until just starting to get tender. &nbsp;Drain. Meanwhile, mix onions, soup, sour cream, salt, and cheese together. &nbsp;Add potatoes and mix well. &nbsp;Pour into greased 13x9 pan. &nbsp;Top with cornflakes and then melted butter. &nbsp;Bake @ 350 for 1 hr.</span></p>

  <p class="Title">Greek Pasta Salad</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T14">From Quick Cooking M/J 2003</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">36 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tri-color spiral pasta&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 med&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomato, cut into thin wedges</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sweet red pepper, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 small&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green pepper, sliced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; crumbled feta cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced black olives, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Dressing:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive or vegetable oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ &nbsp;c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced fresh basil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">9 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; white vinegar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped green onions</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tbl &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated Parmesan cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook pasta; rinse in cold water and drain. &nbsp;Add vegetables and cheese. &nbsp;In blender, combine dressing ingredients; cover and process until smooth. &nbsp;Pour over salad; toss to coat. &nbsp;Cover and refrigerate 2 hours or over night. &nbsp;Toss before serving. &nbsp;Makes 10-12 servings. &nbsp;Has been tripled from original recipe.</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dill weed</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Italian seasoning</span></p>

  <p class="P67"><span class="T1">German Potato Salad</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From A Passion for Potatoes, pg 45</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med onions, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced garlic cloves</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rich chicken stock&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; apple cider vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bacon, cut into ½ inch pieces&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4lb &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; russet potatoes, cut into large cubes</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook potatoes in salted water until tender. &nbsp;Cook bacon until crisp. &nbsp;Add onions &amp; garlic &nbsp;to bacon in skillet and cook until the onions are softened but not browned. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add chicken stock &amp; vinegar. Increase the heat and boil liquids. &nbsp;Set aside.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine &nbsp;potatoes &amp; the onion-bacon dressing. &nbsp;Toss the potato salad with parsley and salt. &nbsp;Taste and correct seasoning. Set aside for at least 1 or 2 hrs before eating, to let the flavors mingle. &nbsp;To serve, invert the potato salad onto a serving platter. &nbsp;Garnish with additional parsley, if desired. &nbsp;Serves 8. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P71">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Hummus</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">32 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chick peas&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ &nbsp;c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; liquid drained from can of chickpeas</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tahini</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sea salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic, crushed</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Drain chickpeas and set aside liquid from can. &nbsp;Combine remaining ingredients in food processor. &nbsp;Add ½ c of liquid from chickpeas. &nbsp;Blend for 3-5 minutes on low until thoroughly mixed and smooth. &nbsp;Place in serving bowl, create a shallow well in the center of the hummus. &nbsp;Add a small amount of olive oil in the well. &nbsp;Garnish with parsley. &nbsp;Serve immediately with fresh, warm pita bread, or cover and refrigerate.</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">OR:</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wash &amp; soak a 1 lb bag of dried chickpeas overnight in UNSALTED water. &nbsp;Next day, pressure cook for 45 minutes on 2</span><span class="T25">nd</span> <span class="T6">red ring with 2 tbl oil added to water. &nbsp;Let cool naturally. &nbsp;Reserve 1 c water and make as above with DOUBLED ingredients.</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; yellow mustard&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; worstershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt to taste</span></p>
