  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Peel eggs and cut in half long-wise. Do not soak eggs to peel, as they retain too much water and become soggy. &nbsp;Separate yolks into bowl. &nbsp;Add all ingredients except paprika to bowl. &nbsp;Blend until very smooth. &nbsp;Fill eggs (you can put filling into plastic bag and snip corner to pipe into eggs easily). &nbsp;Sprinkle with paprika. &nbsp;Keep refrigerated. &nbsp;Makes 20 halves.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From Quick Cooking, J/F 2004</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 8-oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pkg cream cheese, cubed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground nutmeg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; potatoes, peeled and sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">In saucepan, heat milk until bubbles form around sides. &nbsp;Add soups, cream cheese cubes, garlic, nutmeg, and pepper; stir until smooth. &nbsp;Place potatoes and onion in 5 to 6 qt. slow cooker. &nbsp;Pour milk mixture over potato mixture; mix well. &nbsp;Cover and cook on low 6-7 hours or until potatoes are tender. &nbsp;Sprinkle with paprika if desired. &nbsp;Serves 10-12 or more.</p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely chopped garlic, or 1 tbl powder</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Cheese Balls</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P23"><span class="T6">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; softened cream cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated mild cheddar</span></p>
  <p class="P23"><span class="T6">½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated sharp cheddar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Velveeta cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P23"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely diced onion</span></p>
  <p class="P23"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shakes of Liquid Smoke&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Chili powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Using mixer, beat cream cheese until smooth and fluffy. &nbsp;Add cheeses, onion , Worcestershire sauce and Liquid Smoke. &nbsp;Mix until smooth and creamy. &nbsp;Chill.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Shape into 5" x 1" logs and roll in chili powder. &nbsp;Wrap in plastic wrap, put logs into large Ziploc bag and freeze. &nbsp;Will keep for months in the freezer. &nbsp;Defrost the night before eating.</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Hot Crab Dip</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; softened cream cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can flaked crab meat, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced almonds</span></p>
  <p class="P23"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Using hand mixer, beat cream cheese until smooth and fluffy. &nbsp;Add milk, Worcestershire sauce, drained crab meat and onion. Beat until well blended. &nbsp;Pour into greased 1 qt baking dish. &nbsp;Top with almonds and bake at 350 for 15 minutes. &nbsp;Keep warm , serve with crackers.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Fried Okra</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bag of frozen, sliced okra&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1-2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornmeal</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil, for frying&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Defrost okra under warm running water until it isn't too icey. &nbsp;Heat and inch or so of oil in frying pan on medium high heat . &nbsp;Put milk in a bowl and cornmeal mixed with salt in a second bowl. &nbsp;Working in batches, first put okra in milk (separate any that are stuck together), then put them into the cornmeal. &nbsp;Be sure all sides are coated well, then drop them carefully into the hot oil. (To test if oil is hot enough, drop a few crumbs of cornmeal into oil - if it bubbles, the oil is hot enough). &nbsp;Remove okra when golden brown to paper-towel lined pan. &nbsp;Keep this pan in the oven to stay warm as you cook up the other batches. &nbsp;Add more paper towels as needed between layers to absorb grease. &nbsp;Remove those before serving.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cheesy Potato Rounds</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; potatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2+ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; seasoned salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Bake potatoes for 1 hr @400. &nbsp;Remove to cutting board. &nbsp;Slice into ½" slices across the potatoes. &nbsp;Gently place slices onto cookie sheet very close together. &nbsp;Sprinkle slices with seasoned salt and then top with grated cheese. &nbsp;Bake for 15 minutes, or until cheese starts to brown. &nbsp; This is VERY EASY to adjust for more or less servings. &nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Pinto or Black Beans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 ½ - 5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried beans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <ul>
    <li>
      <p class="P49" style="margin-left:3.175cm;"><span class="ListLabel_20_1" style="display:block;float:left;min-width:0.635cm;"></span>Sort &amp; wash beans. &nbsp;Soak overnight in lots of filtered, salted water.<span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
    <li>
      <p class="P49" style="margin-left:3.175cm;"><span class="ListLabel_20_1" style="display:block;float:left;min-width:0.635cm;"></span>Rinse beans well &amp; place in 6 qt crockpot on high.<span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
    <li>
      <p class="P49" style="margin-left:3.175cm;"><span class="ListLabel_20_1" style="display:block;float:left;min-width:0.635cm;"></span>Cover with boiling water to 1" of top of crockpot. Add 3 tbl bacon grease.<span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
    <li>
      <p class="P49" style="margin-left:3.175cm;"><span class="ListLabel_20_1" style="display:block;float:left;min-width:0.635cm;"></span>If using for refried or Mexican beans, add 1 tbl oregano and 1 tbl chili powder.<span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
    <li>
      <p class="P49" style="margin-left:3.175cm;"><span class="ListLabel_20_1" style="display:block;float:left;min-width:0.635cm;"></span>Cook all day. &nbsp;Don't stir often or open crockpot. &nbsp;<span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
    <li>
      <p class="P49" style="margin-left:3.175cm;"><span class="ListLabel_20_1" style="display:block;float:left;min-width:0.635cm;"></span>Salt only when ready to serve. &nbsp;<span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
  </ul>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Fire Salsa</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">32 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; roasted garlic (much &nbsp;less if raw)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cilantro (full amount!)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chipoltes en adobo sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red wine vinegar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Add enough oil to just cover bottom of skillet. &nbsp;Saute onion in skillet until tender. Add ingredients to blender, puree. Makes about 1 qt.</p>
  <p class="P24">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P24">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Chuys Salsa</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 qts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomatillos</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; serranos, whole&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green chiles (or 3 4-oz cans)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cilantro&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 med&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Add all ingredients except salt to large pot, boil 30 min. &nbsp;Strain, saving juice. &nbsp;Now add the salt. &nbsp;Blend solid ingredients, and add back ½ of the strained liquid. &nbsp;Makes nearly 2 qts.</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Guacamole</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ripe avocados&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; regular salsa</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Mash avocados with fork. &nbsp;Stir in salsa. &nbsp;Salt to taste. Serve immediately.</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Everyday Salsa</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; serrano</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cilantro&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder (or 3 cloves)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 30 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Salt to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Blend until smooth. Makes just over 1 qt.</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Tomatillo Avocado Salsa</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomatillos, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; avocado, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; serranos, with seeds&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cilantro</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Puree in blender. &nbsp;Makes 2/3 qt.</p>
  <p class="P24">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Chipolte Tomatillo Salsa</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomatillos, quartered &amp; blackened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chipolte chiles en adobo &amp; sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cilantro&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves roasted garlic&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4-oz cans green chiles</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Blacken tomatillos first. &nbsp;Meanwhile, add other ingredients to blender. &nbsp;Drain tomatillos in colander, add to blender. &nbsp;Puree. &nbsp;Makes about 1 1/3 qts. &nbsp;Five stars!</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Pickled Jalepenos</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Fresh jalapeno peppers&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt per pint</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 clove&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic per pint&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Vinegar and water in equal amounts</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Slice peppers and pack into clean pint canning jars. &nbsp;Add salt and garlic. &nbsp;Cover ingredients with equal amounts of vinegar and water, leaving ¾ inch headspace. &nbsp;Wipe jar rim clean with a damp cloth. &nbsp;Adjust lids and rings; seal. &nbsp;Process 15 minutes in hot-water bath. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Kosher Dill Pickles</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dill seed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; clove of garlic, sliced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/8 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; alum&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 qt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5% vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 qts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; *** this is enough for about 8 qts</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canning &amp; pickling salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Fill quart jars with cucumbers - small whole ones, spears, or slices. &nbsp;Add dill seed, garlic and alum to each. &nbsp;OPTIONAL: &nbsp;1 peppercorn per jar, ¼ pod of hot fresh pepper per jar.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix vinegar, water and salt until salt is dissolved. &nbsp;Fill jar &amp; remove air bubbles, leaving ½" headspace. &nbsp;Water bath for 10 minutes.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Diced Tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wash tomatoes. &nbsp;Skin them by boiling 30 seconds and then plunging into ice water. &nbsp;Cut into quarters, removing stem. &nbsp;Add ½ tsp citric acid and 1 tsp salt to each quart jar. &nbsp;Pack tomatoes into jars, leaving ½" &nbsp;headspace. &nbsp;Ladle hot water over tomatoes, leaving ½" headspace. Remove air bubbles. &nbsp;Process 45 minutes in water bath. &nbsp;(For pints, use ¼ tsp citric acid, ½ tsp salt, and process 40 minutes.)</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Tomato Sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">45 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onions&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; black pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">12 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic, minced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaves</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">citric acid</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wash tomatoes. Remove core end. &nbsp;Cut into quarters. &nbsp;Saute onions &amp; garlic in olive oil in large stockpot. &nbsp;Add tomatoes and seasonings (not citric acid). &nbsp;Simmer 20 minutes. &nbsp;Remove bay leaves. &nbsp;Press sauce through food mill; discard seeds &amp; peels. &nbsp;Cook pulp over</span> <span class="T15">medium</span> <span class="T6">heat until sauce thickens, stirring to prevent burning or sticking. &nbsp;REDUCE VOLUME BY ONE-HALF. &nbsp; Don't rush it!!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add ½ tsp citric acid to each quart jar. &nbsp;Ladle hot sauce into jars, leaving ¼" headspace. &nbsp;Process 40 minutes in water bath. &nbsp;Yields 7 qts. &nbsp;(For pints, use ¼ tsp citric acid per jar and process 35 minutes - yields 14 pints.)</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Peach Halves</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2-3 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peaches, per quart&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Fruit Fresh {1 tsp ascorbic acid per cup water}</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wash peaches. &nbsp;Skin them by boiling 30 seconds and then plunging into ice water. &nbsp;Cut in half. &nbsp;Scrape out aby red fibers (they'll turn brown). &nbsp;Place halves into bowl with Fruit Fresh to prevent browning. &nbsp;Do not keep in this mixture more than 20 minutes. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Make light syrup by cooking sugar &amp; water together. &nbsp;Keep syrup hot.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Pack peaches cavity side down, layers overlaying, into hot jars, leaving ½" headspace. &nbsp;Ladle hot syrup over peaches, leaving ½" headspace. &nbsp;Remove air bubbles. &nbsp;Process pints 25 minutes, quarts 30 minutes, in water bath.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Green Beans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wash &amp; drain beans. &nbsp;Remove strings, trim ends and break or cut into 2-inch pieces. &nbsp;Boil 5 minutes. &nbsp;Add 1 tsp salt to each quart. &nbsp;Pack hot beans into hot jars, leaving 1-inch headspace. &nbsp;Ladle boiling water over beans, leaving 1-inch headspace. &nbsp;Remove air bubbles. &nbsp;Process quarts 25 minutes at 10 lbs pressure in pressure canner. &nbsp;Turn off pressure canner, let pressure return to zero naturally. &nbsp;Wait 2 minutes, then open vent. &nbsp;Unfasten lid; let jars remain in canner 5-10 minutes to adjust to lower temperature. &nbsp;Remove carefully and let cool on towel 2 inches apart for 12-24 hrs.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Strawberry Jam</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped strawberries&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dutch Gel Lite</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Place chopped strawberries into stockpot. &nbsp;Add Dutch Gel Lite and bring mixture to a rolling boil (a boil that does not stop when stirred). &nbsp;STIR CONSTANTLY. &nbsp;Add sugar and return to a rolling boil for 1 minute, stirring constantly. &nbsp;Remove from heat. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Quickly fill pint or half-pint jars to 1/8-inch of tops. &nbsp;Wipe rims and cover quickly with lids. &nbsp;Screw on bands tightly, invert jars for 5 minutes, the turn upright. &nbsp;After 1 hr check seals.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Peach Jam</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peeled peach halves &amp; quarters&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½-1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dutch Gel Lite</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Place peaches into stockpot. &nbsp;Add lemon juice and Dutch Gel Lite and bring mixture to a rolling boil (a boil that does not stop when stirred). &nbsp;STIR CONSTANTLY. &nbsp;Add sugar and return to a rolling boil for 1 minute, stirring constantly. &nbsp;Remove from heat. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Quickly fill pint or half-pint jars to 1/8-inch of tops. &nbsp;Wipe rims and cover quickly with lids. &nbsp;Screw on bands tightly, invert jars for 5 minutes, the turn upright. &nbsp;After 1 hr check seals.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Wild Blackberry Jam</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; blackberries, mashed&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ &nbsp;c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dutch Gel Lite</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Place berries into stockpot. &nbsp;Add water and Dutch Gel Lite and bring mixture to a rolling boil (a boil that does not stop when stirred). &nbsp;STIR CONSTANTLY. &nbsp;Add sugar and return to a rolling boil for 1 minute, stirring constantly. &nbsp;Remove from heat. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Quickly fill pint or half-pint jars to 1/8-inch of tops. &nbsp;Wipe rims and cover quickly with lids. &nbsp;Screw on bands tightly, invert jars for 5 minutes, the turn upright. &nbsp;After 1 hr check seals.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Apple Butter</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">16 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med apples (about 4 lbs)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground cloves</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Wash apples; remove stem and blossom ends; do not peel or core. &nbsp;Cut into small pieces. &nbsp;Add 2 cups water; cover; simmer until apples are soft. &nbsp;Press through food mill. &nbsp;Measure 2 qts apple pulp.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine pulp, sugar, and spices in large baking dish. (Large turkey baking oven). &nbsp;Bake in oven at 225 for 6-8 hrs, or until very thick. &nbsp;Stir often, especially around edges of pan.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Ladle hot butter into hot pint jars, leaving ¼" headspace. &nbsp;Process 10 minutes in hot water bath. &nbsp;Yields about 5 pints.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Rotel Tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">30 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peeled, seeded, squeezed fresh tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">30 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med to large fresh jalapenos, seeded and diced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canning salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients in very large pot; &nbsp;heat until simmering. &nbsp;Put into hot pint jars with ¼ tsp citric acid and ½" headroom. &nbsp;Water bath 15 minutes for pints.</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Hot Stuff</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T26">Justin Wilson Cookbook</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely diced onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely diced fresh Serrano peppers</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine onions &amp; peppers. &nbsp;Fill 5 pint jars with mixture. &nbsp;Add ½ tsp canning salt to each pint. &nbsp;Fill each jar with hot water/vinegar mixture. &nbsp;Leave ½" headspace. &nbsp;Water bath for 15 minutes. &nbsp;Seeding peppers is optional.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P67"><span class="T1">9 Bean Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">4 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried beans (1/2 c of 9 types)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ qt.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boiling water</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 pc&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt pork or ham bone&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 29 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canned, diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Rinse beans and place in crockpot. &nbsp;Add boiling water and salt pork. &nbsp;Simmer 4-8 hours. &nbsp;Remove salt pork and separate meat from fat. &nbsp;Return meat to beans and add remaining ingredients. &nbsp;Simmer 30 minutes or more. &nbsp;Add more cumin if simmering a long time since flavor fades.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serves 10-12. &nbsp;Makes great leftovers - add tomatoes to extend/add liquid. &nbsp;Garnish with lots of sour cream and serve with hot crusty bread.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Potato Leek Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; leeks, chopped **&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lb &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; potato cubes</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med carrot, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; each cumin, coriander, dill, parsley, celery salt</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">6 drops hot sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; yellow squash, diced, if available</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Sauté leeks in olive oil in 6-qt Dutch oven. &nbsp;Add stock, carrots, potatoes, seasonings, and hot pepper sauce. &nbsp;Bring to a boil, then reduce heat, and simmer for 25 to 30 minutes, until vegetables are soft. &nbsp;Blend with blender in Dutch oven until smooth. &nbsp;Serve with garnishes to the side: &nbsp;chives, grated cheddar, sour cream.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">** Leeks can be substituted with 1 yellow onion and the tops of 1 green onion.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Black Bean Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped carrots&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped celery</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onions&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can &nbsp;Rotel tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry sherry&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans Black Beans, undrained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried cilantro&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Polish kielbasa sausage, diced</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add all ingredients to crock pot and cook on LOW 3-5 hours. &nbsp;Serve over steamed rice. &nbsp;Serve garnishes to side: &nbsp;sour cream, chopped green onions, grated cheddar cheese - if desired.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Chopped cooked chicken, ham, or sausage can also be added.</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Restaurant Style Egg Drop Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornstarch</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped fresh chives&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg yolks</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Reserve 1 ½ c of chicken broth and pour the rest into a large saucepan. &nbsp;Stir the salt, ginger and chives into the broth and bring to a rolling boil. &nbsp;In a cup or small bowl, stir together the remaining broth and cornstarch until smooth.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In another bowl, whisk the eggs and egg yolk together using a fork. &nbsp;Add the cornstarch -broth mixture to the soup and keep it boiling. &nbsp;Drizzle egg a little at a time from the folk into the boiling broth mixture. &nbsp;Egg should cook immediately. &nbsp;Serve. &nbsp;Recipe has been doubled.</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Chicken Tortilla Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green bell peppers, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless, skinless chicken breasts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 29 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen corn kernels</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh lime juice</span></p>
  <p class="P30_borderStart"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span><span class="T19">Do not add to</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 12&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn tortillas&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn oil</span></p>
  <p class="P30_borderEnd"><span class="T19">freezer &nbsp;bag!</span><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garnishes, see below</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T22">Entire recipe can be combined in freezer bag and made later (use chicken bouillon cubes now and add 6 c water when cooking).</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Slice chicken into thin strips. Combine everything in crockpot; simmer on HIGH 6-8 hours.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">The garnishes make this dish special! &nbsp;Slice corn tortillas into ¼" strips. &nbsp;Fry in corn oil until crispy; salt lightly. &nbsp;No, tortilla chips from a bag just don't work as well. &nbsp;Place a pile of strips in the bottom of each large bowl for each person. &nbsp;Then add hot soup. &nbsp;On top, add your choice of these garnishes - the more the better!!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Sour cream, grated cheddar cheese, green onions, sliced black olives, cubes of avocado. &nbsp;This is soooo goooood!! &nbsp;The sour cream in the soup makes it very rich (yes, I use plain yogurt some of the time - less fat!).</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T3">Chickpea Chicken Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic clove, minced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rosemary&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt and pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">15oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can diced tomatoes, undrained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped cooked chicken</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tiny pasta shells&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken stock or canned broth</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 16-oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans chickpeas, rinsed and drained</span></p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a large saucepan, heat oil and cook garlic. &nbsp;Stir in tomatoes, chicken, chicken stock, rosemary, and salt and pepper to taste. &nbsp;Simmer 20 minutes.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Meanwhile, cook pasta shells according to package directions. &nbsp;Drain. Put chickpeas in food processor. &nbsp;Ladle in 1 cup of chicken broth. &nbsp;Process until smooth. &nbsp;Return to soup and add cooked shells. &nbsp;Simmer 5 minutes. &nbsp;Serves 6 to 8. &nbsp;Garnish with green onions and/or grated Parmesan cheese, if desired.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Taco Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; browned ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2-28oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2-15oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans corn, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2-15oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans black beans, drained&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2-15oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans kidney beans, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 pkgs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Ranch dressing mix&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 to 8 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; taco seasoning mix</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cube frozen fresh cilantro</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients in large crockpot. &nbsp;Cover and cook on low 4-8 hrs. &nbsp;Serve with tortilla chips, salsa, black olive slices, grated cheddar, chives, and sour cream. &nbsp;</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Hamburger Minestrone Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 lb.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, peeled and sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stalks celery, sliced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">29 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cabbage, shredded</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaf&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; basil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T7">2 potatoes, peeled, cubed &nbsp; &nbsp;-</span> <span class="T20">Don't add to freezer bag</span> <span class="T7">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P46">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Brown meat and drain. &nbsp;Combine all ingredients into crockpot. Add water to cover well. &nbsp;Cook on LOW 8-12 hours (or HIGH 4-6 hours). Serve with Parmesan cheese. &nbsp;Serves 6, or about 3 quarts.</span></p>
  <p class="P16">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T22">Great for using up leftover veggies. &nbsp;May be combined without potatoes and water for freezing for later. &nbsp;Never freeze potatoes - they turn mush-y.</span></p>

  <p class="P18">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T3">Spiced Lentil Soup with Beef</span></p>
  <p class="P11">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lentils</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; medium onions, finely chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lg cloves garlic, finely chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground beef&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lg bay leaves</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med carrots, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lg celery ribs, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground cumin</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">28oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canned diced tomatoes, with juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground coriander</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 Qts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P6">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In 6- to 8-qt pot, combine olive oil, onions, and beef. &nbsp;Cook, until onions are translucent and meat has lost its raw color.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add carrots and celery and continue to saute. &nbsp;Stir in tomatoes with all their juices, water, lentils, garlic, bay leaves, parsley, cumin, coriander, cinnamon, and salt. &nbsp;Cover and bring to a boil.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Reduce heat and simmer steadily, partially covered, stirring occasionally, for 1 ½ to 2 hours, until the lentils are very tender.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add lemon juice. &nbsp;Taste and correct with salt. &nbsp;Add more water, if necessary, to bring the soup to desired consistency; it should be thick.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">OPTIONS</span><span class="T6">: &nbsp;Can also be made with chicken or lamb.</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Barley Beef Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stew meat&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; med carrots, peeled and chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; rib celery, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lg mushrooms, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 14oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes, with juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken/beef broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pearl barley</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">pinch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper, to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add all to large crockpot, except barley. &nbsp;Cook on high 4-8 hrs. &nbsp;Add barley last 2 hours of cooking.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P14"><span class="T4">Lentil &amp; Brown Rice Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lentils, rinsed and picked over&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cloves garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; long grain brown rice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; basil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 to 6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaf&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">35 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Italian-style diced tomatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Add later</span><span class="T6">:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cider vinegar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh parsley, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt and pepper to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a large stockpot, combine first set of ingredients; bring to a boil. Reduce heat, cover and simmer 45-55 minutes, stirring occasionally, until rice and lentils are tender. Remove bay leaf. Stir in vinegar, salt, pepper, and parsley. &nbsp;Thin soup with hot broth, if necessary. Makes 8-10 servings.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Soup Beans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried pinto beans, sorted &amp; washed</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chili powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 pc&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt pork (not sliced)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bay leaves</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Soak beans in salted water overnight. &nbsp;Drain &amp; wash thoroughly. &nbsp;Place in roaster oven with spices, onions and salt pork. &nbsp;Cover all with water 1" above beans. &nbsp;Cook all day starting at 350 and reducing to 225 once beans are tender. &nbsp;Remove salt pork and let cool. &nbsp;Remove meat from salt pork piece and return the meat to the soup beans. &nbsp;Salt to taste and remove bay leaves before serving. &nbsp;Serve with cornbread! &nbsp;Makes a lot - serves family of 8 for two suppers.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Tomato Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 14-oz cans diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced celery</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh basil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Whipping cream</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onions</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a Dutch oven, cook onions, celery, and garlic in olive oil until onions are translucent. &nbsp;Add tomatoes, don't drain. &nbsp;Fill each can ¼ up with water and rinse out the can into the soup pot. &nbsp;Add basil and salt; bring to a boil. &nbsp;Reduce heat and simmer for 20 minutes, stirring occasionally. &nbsp; Remove from heat. &nbsp;Using a plunger blender, puree soup in the Dutch oven being careful not to splatter the hot soup on yourself. &nbsp;Return to low heat until ready to serve. &nbsp;Serve with cream and sliced green onions as garnish. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cheddar Cheese Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onions, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stalks celery, sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, finely grated</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 14oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans potato/leek soup (not creamy)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">14 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can cream of mushroom soup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hard shakes of garlic Tabasco sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Sauté onions, celery, and carrots in margarine in 4-qt Dutch oven. &nbsp;Add chicken broth and simmer 30 minutes. &nbsp;Add soups, cheese, Tabasco sauce, sour cream, and salt &amp; pepper to taste. &nbsp;Simmer 15 minutes or more, but do not let it boil! &nbsp;Serves 10-12.</span></p>

  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Beer-Cheese Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2-12oz cans&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; beer</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped celery&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whole milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peeled, diced potatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; black pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; paprika</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In 6-qt stock pot, sauté onions and celery in butter until soft. &nbsp;Add beer, broth, and potatoes. &nbsp;Bring to a boil; reduce heat, cover, and simmer 10-15 minutes or until potatoes are tender.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Puree soup with plunger-style mixer until smooth. &nbsp;Add cheese, salt, pepper, and paprika. &nbsp;Stir until cheese is melted. &nbsp;Add milk and reduce heat to medium-low - don't let it boil! &nbsp;Ready to serve when thoroughly heated. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">We love it served in individual round, sour-dough bread loaves that are hollowed out as bowls. &nbsp;</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">John Barleycorn's Cheese Soup</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Linda Gildner</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Velveeta cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped fine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, chopped fine</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery stalks, chopped fine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 gal&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken bouillon cubes</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Boil water. &nbsp;Add vegetables and chicken bouillon cubes. &nbsp;Cook for 10 minutes. &nbsp;Add diced Velveeta cheese. &nbsp;Stir until cheese melts. &nbsp;Make a roux with butter and flour. &nbsp;Mix into soup.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Kentucky Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry soup mix&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 16c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water or broth</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; carrots, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; celery stalks, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 qts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cooked chicken, diced</span></p>

  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add all ingredients to crockpot and cook all day. &nbsp;</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Chicken &amp; Andouille Gumbo</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bacon drippings, lard, or oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless chicken breast&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; andouille sausage, sliced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">5 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped onion&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onion</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped bell pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped celery</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10 cloves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, minced</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 qts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken stock&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt, pepper, hot sauce to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">First, chop your vegetables and put your stock in a pot on a back burner to warm.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Now, in BOTTOM PART OF PRESSURE COOKER make a nice dark roux to the dark chocolate stage (about 45-50 minutes). &nbsp;Add onions, bell pepper and celery, stirring vigorously all the while. &nbsp;Continue to stir the roux, and after a few minutes add your chopped scallions and parsley. &nbsp;Once the onions are nearly transparent, add the minced garlic to the roux. &nbsp;After a minute or two more of energetic stirring, start blending in the hot stock - one cup at a time. &nbsp;Let each addition of stock be absorbed into the roux before adding more. &nbsp;It will take you several minutes at least to add the stock in this way. &nbsp;Reduce the heat to a simmer and add the andouille. &nbsp;Cut the chicken into small bite-size pieces and add to the gumbo.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">After 15-20 minutes, start cooking your rice. &nbsp;Taste the gumbo and adjust the seasonings to your liking. &nbsp;Serve hot over rice with crusty bread. &nbsp;Freezes and reheats well. &nbsp;</span><span class="T15">This recipe has been doubled from the original.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Creamy Chicken Tortilla Soup</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Linda Gildner</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 cloves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic, minced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boneless chicken breasts - cooked</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onion, chopped&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cumin</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 pkg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; taco seasoning</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">42 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped fresh cilantro</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream of chicken soup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; half and half</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh sals&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; a&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; creamed corn</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Tortilla chips</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large pot, sauté garlic and onion in butter for 5 minutes. &nbsp;Add flour and stir well, cooking for 1 minute more. &nbsp;Add broth and half and half. &nbsp;Bring to a boil and reduce heat to low. &nbsp;Add soup, salsa, corn, chicken, cumin, taco seasoning and 2 tbl cilantro. &nbsp;Stir and continue to heat for 15 minutes. &nbsp;The soup can be held in a 6 ½ qt crockpot on low at this point.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Serve over bowlfuls of crumbled tortilla chips. &nbsp;Top with cheese, avocado chunks, black olives, green onion slices, cilantro, whatever! &nbsp;Makes 6 qts of very yummy soup.</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Lemon Chicken &amp; Rice Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">9 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uncooked, long-grain rice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cooked chicken, diced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried lemon peel</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dried dill</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whole milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt &amp; pepper to taste</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large pot bring broth to a strong simmer. &nbsp;Add rice; cover and cook 5 minutes, stirring occasionally. &nbsp;Reduce heat &nbsp;and add the remaining ingredients. &nbsp; Recipe has been tweaked and doubled from original.</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Olive Garden Minestrone Soup</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced onions</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced celery&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; minced garlic</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">8 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; veg. or chicken broth&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 30-oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can red kidney beans, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">28 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; diced tomatoes (not drained)&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 30-oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can small white beans, drained</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thinly sliced carrots&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oregano&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; basil</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; thyme&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hot water</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dijon mustard&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; red wine</span></p>
  <p class="P25"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; small shell pasta&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; box of frozen chopped spinach</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large pot, sauté garlic, onion, celery in oil until onions begin to turn translucent. &nbsp;Add broth to pot and tomatoes, beans, carrots, hot water, mustard, and spices. &nbsp;Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and allow to simmer for 20 minutes. &nbsp;. &nbsp;Add spinach, wine and pasta and cook for an additional 20 minutes or until desired consistency. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P28"><span class="T3">&nbsp;Sour Cream Scones</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raisins&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 tsp.&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine ingredients in mixer to make a soft dough. Divide into 3 balls, flour, roll out into circles, cut into 8 pieces with pizza cutter. Bake at 375º on cookie sheet till golden brown, about 15 minutes. &nbsp;Brush top of scones with butter. &nbsp;These are great to freeze and reheat later for breakfast! &nbsp;Makes 24.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P60"><span class="T1">Warm Old-Fashioned&nbsp;Peach Cake</span></p>
  <p class="P38"><span class="T28">Cut up 1 stick of BUTTER into a 9x13 pan.&nbsp; Put this in oven and preheat to 350.&nbsp; While it's preheating, mix together:</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whole or low-fat milk</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P38"><span class="T28">Stir together until smooth.&nbsp; Pour batter over melted butter.&nbsp; Then arrange on top:</span></p>
  <p class="P38"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span><span class="T28">1 16oz pkg frozen sliced peaches - not defrosted</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp;</span><span class="T28">Bake for 1 hour or until golden brown in center.&nbsp;If cooking 2, allow 1 hour 15 minutes. &nbsp;Serve warm with whipped cream, if desired.&nbsp; Makes 12 servings. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P26">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P26">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Hummingbird Cake</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; crushed pineapple, don't drain</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bananas, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nuts, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">Mix flour, sugar, salt, baking soda, and cinnamon together. Stir in oil and eggs until dry ingredients are just moist. &nbsp;Add pineapple and bananas, stirring until blended. Do not beat. &nbsp;Blend in nuts. Bake in greased and floured pan at 350: three 9-inch round pans, 25-30 minutes; one 9 x 13 pan, 40-45 minutes; one 10-inch tube pan, 1 hour. &nbsp;Cake is done when toothpick inserted in center comes out clean. Cool and frost.</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Gingerbread Cake</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coconut oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; molasses</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; buttermilk</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P65"><span class="T18">Blend sugar, oil and eggs together in mixing bowl. &nbsp;Stir in molasses. &nbsp;Combine dry ingredients and add with buttermilk. &nbsp;Beat well. &nbsp;Pour into a well greased and floured 9x13 pan. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 30-35 minutes.</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Blueberry Coffee Cake</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream cheese, softened</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh or frozen blueberries</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">Cream butter, cream cheese and sugar. &nbsp;Add eggs, vanilla, milk, flour, baking powder &amp; soda, salt and berries. &nbsp;Mix and spread in a &nbsp;9x13 pan.</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T29">&nbsp;TOPPING:</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cold butter</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">Cut in butter to dry topping ingredients and sprinkly on coffee cake. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 30-35 min.</span></p>

  <p class="Title">Morning Glory Muffins</p>
  <p class="P58"><span class="T12">Taste of Home, A/M 2000</span></p>
  <p class="P61">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whole wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oat bran</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; unsweetened applesauce</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vegetable oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; molasses</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; orange extract</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; finely grated carrots&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raisins</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; walnut pieces&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coconut flakes, sweetened</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 med&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tart apple, peeled &amp; finely chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">In a bowl, combine dry ingredients. &nbsp;In another bowl, combine eggs, applesauce, oil, molasses, and extracts; mix well. &nbsp;Stir into the dry ingredients just until moistened. &nbsp;Fold in carrots, raisins, walnuts, coconut, and apple. &nbsp;Fill paper-lined muffin cups three-fourths full. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 25-30 minutes or until toothpick comes out clean. &nbsp;Cool for 5 minutes before removing from pans to wire racks. &nbsp;Makes about 2 dozen. &nbsp;Great served warm!</span></p>

  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Salvation Army Donuts</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3/8 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lard</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; small can evaporated milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; small can water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ¾ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nutmeg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cream lard and sugar until fluffy. &nbsp;Beat eggs, add milk and water. &nbsp;Add liquid to creamed mixture. Mix flour, baking powder, salt and nutmeg together. &nbsp;Add to other mixture. &nbsp;Add enough flour to mae a stif dough. &nbsp;Roll and cut. &nbsp;Fry in more lard. &nbsp;Makes about 5 dozen.</span></p>
