  <p class="P64">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Sour Cream Coffee Cake</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Topping:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; packed brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped walnuts or pecans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cake:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft wheat flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Blend topping ingredients together, set aside.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cream butter and sugar in mixing bowl. &nbsp;Add eggs, sour cream and vanilla and mix well. &nbsp;Combine dry ingredients well in separate bowl. &nbsp;Add to creamed mixture. &nbsp;Beat until combined. Pour half of the batter into a greased 9x13 pan. &nbsp;Sprinkle with half of the topping. &nbsp;Add remaining batter, and then topping. &nbsp;Bake at 325 for 40-50 minutes or until cake tests done.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Uncle Gary's World Famous Cheesecake</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; graham cracker crumbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; melted butter</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">24 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream cheese, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">dash&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <ol>
    <li>
      <p class="P50" style="margin-left:3.6619cm;"><span style="display:block;float:left;min-width:1.1219cm;">3</span><span class="T6">eggs</span><span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine crust ingredients and press into bottom of spring form pan. &nbsp;Refrigerate.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a mixer, combine cream cheese, sugar, salt and vanilla. &nbsp;Beat well until very smooth. &nbsp;Add eggs, one at a time, beating thoroughly after each addition. &nbsp;Pour cream cheese mixture onto crust and bake undisturbed in preheated 350 oven for 1 hour 10 minutes. &nbsp;Then check to see that the top has a nice even tan color across the top. &nbsp;Bake a little longer if necessary.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Remove from oven and increase oven temp to 450. &nbsp;Combine topping ingredients, spread on cake and return to oven for 10 minutes. &nbsp;Refrigerate until well chilled before removing from pan. &nbsp; The longer it can stay in the fridge (1 or 2 days) the denser the cake will be when you cut it.</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P66"><span class="T1">Lemon Poppy Seed Loaf</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; poppy seeds</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated lemon zest&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon extract</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; applesauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg whites</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Glaze:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Beat egg whites till soft peaks form and set aside. &nbsp; In large bowl, mix flour, seeds, lemon zest, baking powder and baking soda. &nbsp;In another large bowl, combine sugar oil, applesauce sour cream and lemon juice. &nbsp;Stir this mixture into the flour mixture then fold in egg whites. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Pour into 2 greased 10" loaf pans and bake at 350 for 45-50 minutes or until toothpick inserted comes out clean. &nbsp;Cool in pan for 10 minutes before removing to rack. &nbsp;Mix glaze and pour over loaf. &nbsp;Cool, slice, and serve.</span></p>
  <p class="P5">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P67"><span class="T1">Easy Peanut Butter Cookies</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; peanut butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">3/4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Stir all ingredients until combined. &nbsp;Shape level tablespoonfuls into balls. &nbsp;Place 2" apart on baking sheets lined with parchment paper. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 16 minutes. &nbsp;Cool for 5 minutes; remove to wire racks. &nbsp;Makes about 2 dzn.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">VARIATION</span><span class="T6">: &nbsp;For light and cake-like cookies, use 4 eggs rather than 2. &nbsp;Thin batter, but bakes up very light.</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grandma's Danish Pastries</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg, separated&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pinch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; jelly of your choice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; crushed nuts of your choice</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; or maraschino cherries</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">Cream butter and sugar together. &nbsp;Add egg yolk, vanilla, salt, and flour. &nbsp;Mix well. &nbsp;Roll into 1" balls and place on wax paper. &nbsp;Beat egg white lightly. &nbsp;Dip each ball into egg white and then into the crushed nuts. &nbsp;When coated completely, place onto ungreased cookie sheet. &nbsp;When all balls have been coated in nuts, press a hole into the center of each (don't go thru to the bottom, though!). &nbsp;Fill each hole with jelly or cherry. &nbsp;Do not fill too full as jelly will melt and run when it cooks. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 10-12 minutes. &nbsp;Cool before serving. &nbsp;Makes 24. &nbsp;**Three batches fits in Bosch mixer!!**</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T2">Pecan Pie Bars</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">Taste of Home, F/M 2004</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cold butter (not margarine)</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">FILLING:</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn syrup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, melted</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pecans</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">In large bowl, combine flour, sugar and salt with whisk. Cut in butter until crumbly. &nbsp;Press onto the bottom and sides of greased 15x10x1-in. pan. Bake at 350 for 18-22 minutes or until crust edges are beginning to brown and bottom is set.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">For filling, combine eggs, sugar, corn syrup, butter and vanilla in a large bowl; mix well. Stir in pecans - chopped or whole, your choice. &nbsp;Have filling ready when crust is finished cooking. &nbsp;Pour filling over crust QUICKLY and return to oven. &nbsp;Bake 25-30 minutes longer or until edges are firm and center is almost set. &nbsp;Cool on wire rack. &nbsp;Cut into bars. &nbsp;Makes 3-4 dozen. &nbsp;This recipe has been HALVED from the original which called for double all ingredients and 2 pans. &nbsp;Cooking times are the same. &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Spiced Pumpkin Bars</span></p>
  <p class="P58"><span class="T12">Taste of Home, A/M 2000</span></p>
  <p class="P63">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground nutmeg</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground cloves&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">15oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can pumpkin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; unsweetened applesauce</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">In a bowl, combine dry ingredients, mixing well. In another bowl, combine eggs, pumpkin and applesauce; mix well. &nbsp;You may need to use a whisk to blend completely. &nbsp;Stir wet ingredients into the dry ingredients. &nbsp;Spread into a greased 15x10x1 jelly roll pan as evenly as possible - it won't flatten or spread as it cooks. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 25-30 minutes, making sure center is done. &nbsp;Cool on a wire rack before cutting into bars. &nbsp;Dust with confectioners' sugar, if desired. &nbsp;Serve with whipped topping and it tastes like pumpkin pie cake! &nbsp;Makes 30 bars. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Ginger-Oatmeal Cookies</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Southern Living, Oct 2002</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; quick-cooking oats</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raisins&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; melted butter or margarine</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; molasses&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped walnuts</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hot water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, lightly beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Combine flour, baking soda, salt, oats, raisins, sugar, and ginger in large bowl; add butter, molasses, walnuts, hot water, and eggs. &nbsp;Stir until blended. &nbsp;Divide dough into 2" balls. &nbsp;Place at least 3" apart on greased cookie sheets; flatten each ball to ¼" thickness. &nbsp;Brush tops with water and sprinkle evenly with sugar. &nbsp;Bake at 375 for 10-12 minutes. &nbsp;Makes about 3 dozen.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">White Chocolate Cranberry Bars</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; firmly packed brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cranberries, halved</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped walnuts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; white vanilla chops</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Grease 13x9 baking pan. &nbsp;In large bowl, combine flour, baking soda and baking powder. &nbsp;In another bowl, combine brown sugar, sugar and butter; beat until light and fluffy. &nbsp;Add eggs 1 at a time, beating well after each addition. &nbsp;Add vanilla; blend well. &nbsp;Gradually add flour mixture; blend at low speed just until combined. &nbsp;Fold in cranberries, walnuts, and vanilla chips. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Spread batter in greased pan. &nbsp;Bake for 30-40 minutes, until golden. &nbsp;Cool 1 hour or until completely cooled. Cut into bars. &nbsp;Yields 36 bars.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Sour Cream Sugar Cookies</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shortening&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine shortening, 1 c sugar, egg &amp; vanilla; cream till light and fluffy. &nbsp;Combine flour, baking soda &amp; salt in separate bowl. &nbsp;Blend flour mixture into creamed mixture. &nbsp;Stir in sour cream.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Roll dough into 1" balls; place on parchment lined cookie sheet. &nbsp;Flatten slightly with fork &amp; sprinkle with sugar. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 10-12 minutes.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Almond Fingers</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Southern Living Cookbook, pg 84</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg yolks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; almond extract&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all purpose flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 400. &nbsp;Beat butter &nbsp;until creamy; gradually add sugar. &nbsp;Add yolks one at a time; stir in extracts. &nbsp;Combine flour &amp; slat; add to butter mixture; beating well. &nbsp;Sift powdered sugar over work surface. &nbsp;Shape 1 tbl dough into 2 ½ inch log; repeat with remaining dough. &nbsp;Place on parchment lined cookie sheet.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg white, lightly beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground almonds</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; semisweet chocolate&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; white chocolate</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Brush each cookie log with egg white and lightly sprinkle with almonds. &nbsp;Bake at 400 for 9 to 10 minutes or until barely browned. &nbsp;Remove cookies to wire racks to cool completely.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Melt chocolates in separate pans - stir often to check! &nbsp;Dip ends of cookies into melted chocolate, covering about half the cookie. Sprinkle ends with more ground almonds. &nbsp;Place cookies on wire racks until chocolate is firm. &nbsp;Yields 44-46 using 1 oz cookie scoop. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">NOTE: &nbsp;Make double batch for Christmas.</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Lemon Bars</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Southern Living Cookbook, pg 89</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all purpose flour, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar, divided</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cold butter, cut up&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine 2 cups flour and ½ c powdered sugar. &nbsp;Cut butter into flour mixture with a pastry blender until mixture is crumbly. &nbsp;Spoon flour mixture into a 13x9 pan; press into pan evenly and firmly, using fingertips. Bake at 350 for 20-25 minutes or until lightly browned.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine ½ c flour and baking powder; set aside. &nbsp;Combine eggs, 1 c sugar, and lemon juice; beat well. &nbsp;Stir dry ingredients into egg mixture, and pour over baked crust. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 22-25 minutes or until lightly browned and set. &nbsp;Cool on a wire rack. &nbsp;Sprinkle with ¼ c powdered sugar and cut into bars. &nbsp;Yields 2 dozen.</span></p>

  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Vanilla Wafers</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sticks butter, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">10.5 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft-wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cream butter and sugar. &nbsp;Add eggs and beat until fluffy. &nbsp;Combine dry ingredients and whisk to mix well. &nbsp;Add to creamed mixture. &nbsp;Beat until smooth. Drop by tablespoon full 2 inches or more apart onto parchment-lined baking sheet. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 7-8 minutes or until edges are golden brown. &nbsp;Remove to wire rack to cool. &nbsp;Makes 440+. &nbsp;VERY YUMMY - especially in homemade banana pudding!!</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Chocolate Peanut Butter Squares</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stick butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; creamy unsweetened peanut butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; graham cracker crumbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <ol>
    <li>
      <p class="P48" style="margin-left:3.81cm;"><span style="display:block;float:left;min-width:1.27cm;">1</span><span class="T6">stick butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; semi-sweet chocolate chips&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span> <span class="odfLiEnd"></span>&nbsp;</p>
    </li>
  </ol>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Melt 1 stick of butter in medium saucepan over low heat. &nbsp;Stir in sugar until dissolved. &nbsp;Add peanut butter and stir until smooth. &nbsp;Add crumbs and mix well. &nbsp;Remove from heat. &nbsp;This will make a stiff "dough." &nbsp;Spread dough in a lightly greased 13x9 pan. &nbsp;Press down evenly.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Melt remaining stick of butter; add chocolate chips and keep heat very low. &nbsp;When chocolate is soft, stir gently. &nbsp;Continue heating until lumps are all melted. &nbsp;Stir and then spread this mixture over the peanut butter layer. &nbsp;Refrigerate until chocolate is firm. &nbsp;Store in fridge.</span></p>
  <p class="P66"><span class="T1">Chess Squares</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sticks butter, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 16 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; light brown sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft-wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped nuts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cream butter and sugars until fluffy. &nbsp;Add 4 eggs. &nbsp;Combine dry ingredients and whisk to mix well. &nbsp;Add to creamed mixture. &nbsp;Beat until smooth. &nbsp;Add nuts. &nbsp;Pour into greased 9x13 pan and bake at 350 for 30 minutes. &nbsp;Cool before cutting.</span></p>
  <p class="P39">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Hello Dolly Cookies</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In 13x9 pan, layer the following:</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stick butter, melted&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; graham cracker crumbs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shredded, sweetened coconut</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped pecans</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; semi-sweet chocolate chips</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sweetened condensed milk</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook 30 minutes at 350. &nbsp;Cool before cutting.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Oatmeal Drop Cookies</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shortening&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; molasses</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oats&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped &nbsp;pecans</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; semi-sweet chocolate chips</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix shortening, sugar, eggs, &amp; molasses. &nbsp;Stir dry ingredients together &amp; blend in. &nbsp;Stir in oats, nuts &amp; chocolate chips.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Drop by tsp on parchment paper-lined cookie sheet. &nbsp;Bake 6 minutes at 400. &nbsp;Makes 50-60.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Mississippi Mud</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Grandma Norris</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 sticks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cocoa powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/8 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped nuts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; miniature marshmallows</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. Melt butter and cocoa together in large pan. &nbsp;Remove from heat &amp; stir in sugar and beaten eggs; mix well. &nbsp;Add flour, salt, nuts and vanilla, mixing well. &nbsp;Spoon batter into greased 13x9 pan. &nbsp;Bake 35-45 minutes. &nbsp;Sprinkle marshmallows on hot cake. &nbsp;Return to oven 5 minutes to melt. &nbsp;Cover with frosting.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">*** &nbsp;You can make unfrosted brownies with the bottom layer if you stop before adding the marshmallows and let cool. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T15">Frosting:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cocoa powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients. Mix until smooth. &nbsp;Spread on hot cake. (Sugar in frosting has been reduced from original of 3 cups.)</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Nanc's Favorite Lemon Bars</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">CRUST:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 sticks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, softened</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Blend crust ingredients and press into 13x9 pan. Bake crust for 20-25 minutes until the edges just atart to turn golden brown.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">FILLING:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 lg&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon extract&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Whisk all ingredients together and pour onto baked crust. &nbsp;Bake an additional 25 minutes. &nbsp;Let cool and sprinkle with powdered sugar. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Cream Cheese Frosting</span></p>
  <p class="P35">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream cheese, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 lb box&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; powdered sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; margarine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T28">&nbsp;Mix cream cheese and butter. Add sugar and vanilla. Beat until smooth. &nbsp;This makes a lot of frosting, but is freezes well, if you have extra. &nbsp;Makes 1 cake, either triple-layer, sheet or bundt.</span></p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P34">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Nut Crunch Topping</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In food processor bowl with knife, pulse together &nbsp;JUST until butter is in small pieces:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 stick&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Pour into 13x9 pan and mix well with:</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped nuts (reuse food processor bowl for chopping nuts)</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Bake 15 minutes at 400. &nbsp;Cool completely, then freeze. &nbsp;Serve over fruit.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Heavenly Hot Fudge</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 squares&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;unsweetened chocolate&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 stick&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">pinch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">13 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; evaporated milk</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Melt chocolate &amp; butter &amp; salt in top of double boiler. &nbsp;Start adding sugar slowly, stirring constantly. &nbsp;When all sugar is blended, add milk slowly, stirring constantly. &nbsp;Stir until satiny and smooth &amp; not grainy. &nbsp;Store in refrigerator in qt jar.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Lemon Butter</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 stick&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, well beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon peel</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Melt butter &amp; sugar &amp; lemon until smooth. &nbsp;Add beaten eggs slowly, beating constantly. &nbsp;With rubber spatula, scrap sides &amp; stir continuously until thick as cream. &nbsp;Makes 1 pint. &nbsp;Keep in fridge. &nbsp;Will keep for months. From Grandma Saenz.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Haystacks</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; evaporated milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn syrup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coconut&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix in 4-qt sauce pan. Cook all except coconut &amp; vanilla. &nbsp;Cook over low heat till sugar dissolves. &nbsp;Bring to a boil over med heat; stir often. &nbsp;Cook to soft ball stage (use candy thermometer!). &nbsp;Remove from heat and add vanilla &amp; coconut. &nbsp;Mix well. &nbsp;Shape quickly into balls or cones. &nbsp;Place on waxed paper. &nbsp;Makes 36-45.</span></p>
  <p class="P34"></p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Butter Pie Crust</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 stick&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; frozen butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ice water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Put flour &amp; salt in food processor (knife in place). &nbsp;Add butter in 6-8 pieces. &nbsp;Process 20-30 seconds. &nbsp;Add water through chute while running processor. &nbsp;Process 20-30 seconds until ball forms. &nbsp;AS SOON AS BALL FORMS - STOP! &nbsp;Makes 2 crusts.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Graham Cracker Pie Crust</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; graham cracker crumbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; melted butter</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Combine in mixing bowl until butter is well distributed. &nbsp;Press mixture into 9-inch pie pan, covering sides &amp; bottom. &nbsp;Use small Pyrex bowl to push crumbs in evenly. &nbsp;Refrigerate 10 minutes.</span></p>

  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Blueberry Pear Cobbler</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From Taste of Home, July/Aug 2002</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2-15oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cans sliced pears&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter or margarine, cubed</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">19oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pkg blueberry muffin mix with 2 cans of real blueberries</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Drain pears, reserving ¾ c juice. &nbsp;Pour pears and reserved juice into a greased 2-qt baking dish. &nbsp;Sprinkle with ½ of the muffin mix; top with one drained can of blueberries and &nbsp;dot with butter. &nbsp;Bake, uncovered, at 400 for 20-25 minutes or until bubbly and top is lightly browned. &nbsp;Save other half of muffin mix and 2</span><span class="T25">nd</span> <span class="T6">can for next time! &nbsp;Serve 6-8 with ice cream.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Traditional Pumpkin Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">15 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can pumpkin&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 14 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; canned sweetened condensed milk</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, slightly beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ground ginger&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nutmeg</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 9" unbaked pie crust</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 425. In a large bowl, combine filling ingredients, mixing well. &nbsp;Pour into pie crust. Bake 15 minutes at 425. Reduce oven temp to 350 and continue baking 35 to 40 minutes for until knife inserted in center comes out clean. Cool pie before cutting. Refrigerate any leftovers.</span></p>

  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Grandma Norris' Pecan Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, melted&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pecans</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn syrup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dash&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Beat eggs, add sugar. &nbsp;Stir in corn syrup, pecans, melted butter and salt. &nbsp;Mix well. &nbsp;Pour into 9" unbaked pie shell. &nbsp;Bake 45 minutes.</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T2">Philadelphia Cream Cheese Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; graham cracker crumb crust</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">12 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream cheese, softened&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon peel&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cream together cream cheese and sugar. &nbsp;Add eggs one at a time, mixing until smooth. Stir in lemon juice &amp; peel. &nbsp;Pour mixture into crust. &nbsp;Bake 30 minutes at 325 or until filling is set &amp; firm.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine sour cream, lemon juice and sugar &amp; mix until smooth. &nbsp;After shell &amp; filling have cooled 5 minutes, pour on sour cream topping &amp; spread evenly. &nbsp;Return to oven for ONLY 5 minutes.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">For best results, refrigerate completed pie over night.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Key Lime Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">14 oz &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sweetened condensed milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg yolks</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; key lime juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; graham cracker crust</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Mix filling ingredients and pour into crust. &nbsp;Bake for 15 minutes. &nbsp;Allow to stand 10 minutes before refrigerating. &nbsp;Chill completely before serving.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Strawberry-Cream Cheese Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">9"&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baked pie crust&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cream cheese, softened</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine until smooth; spread on pie crust.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 pts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced fresh strawberries&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 pt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MASHED fresh strawberries</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornstarch</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Place sliced berries on cream cheese mixture, cut side down. &nbsp;Mix mashed berries (mash with potato masher) with lemon juice, cornstarch, and sugar; cook over med-high heat until mixture boils and begins to thicken, stirring constantly. &nbsp;Cool and pour into pie shell; refrigerate 4-6 hrs. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">NOTE: &nbsp;I always need to make 2 of these. &nbsp;I don't double the sugar in the cooked mixture.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P67"><span class="T1">Lime Jello Salad</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">6 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Lime Jello package&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 7-Up or Sprite</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boiling water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 20 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; crushed pineapple</span></p>
  <p class="P15"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; small marshmallows&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bananas, cut up</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Drain pineapple and save juice. &nbsp;Dissolve Jello in water. &nbsp;Mix well and add 7-Up, pineapple, bananas, and marshmallows. &nbsp;Pour into 13x9 pan and chill until jelled.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T16">Topping</span><span class="T6">:1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg, beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornstarch&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pineapple juice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Cool Whip&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Beat egg and add juice, sugar, lemon juice, and cornstarch. &nbsp;Cook over low heat until thick.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cool - add cheese, Cool Whip, and sour cream. &nbsp;Put on top of jello. &nbsp; Keep refrigerated.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Vanilla Pudding</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs yolks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Mix sugar, flour &amp; salt in top of double boiler. &nbsp;Stir in milk. &nbsp;Cook over boiling water 15 minutes. &nbsp;Remove from heat and add egg yolks, beating after each. &nbsp;Cook 5 minutes more. &nbsp;Add vanilla. &nbsp;Chill.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Tapioca Pudding</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 qts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; instant tapioca</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">In 8 qt stockpot, combine all ingredients. &nbsp;Let sit 5 minutes, then bring to a ROLLING boil while stirring CONSTANTLY. &nbsp;Remove from heat, stir until not foamy on top. &nbsp;Add 1 tsp vanilla extract. &nbsp;Let cool 20 minutes; refrigerate 4-6 hours or until cold.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Rice Pudding</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cooked long-grain rice&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; raisins&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon peel&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon juice</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; melted butter</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Combine all ingredients in large mixing bowl. &nbsp;When well mixed, pour into a greased 2-qt baking dish. &nbsp;Bake at 375 for 50 minutes or until set. &nbsp;Serve warm. &nbsp;Makes 8-10 servings.</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Chess Pie</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; corn meal</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; melted butter</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk or cream&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Mix gently. &nbsp;Do not over beat eggs. &nbsp;Pour in unbaked pie crust and bake in 350 oven for 40-50 minutes or until it doesn't shake. &nbsp;You make have to cut the temperature down to 325.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">VARIATIONS:</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Lemon Chess Pie: &nbsp; Omit vanilla and add ¼ cup lemon juice,</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Pineapple Chess Pie: &nbsp;Add 1 small can pineapple, drained to above recipe.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Banana Pudding</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">6&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs yolks&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla wafers&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ripe bananas</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Mix sugar, flour &amp; salt in top of double boiler. &nbsp;Stir in milk. &nbsp;Cook over boiling water 15 minutes. &nbsp;Remove from heat and add egg yolks, beating after each. &nbsp;Cook 5 minutes more. &nbsp;Add vanilla. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Make layers of cookies, banana slices, pudding - repating layers. Chill. &nbsp;Top with whipped cream. &nbsp;</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">&nbsp;Granola</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 -18oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; round canisters of oats (=12 c)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shredded coconut&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; honey</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; warm water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced almonds</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; almond extract</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix the dry ingredients together, breaking up lumps of coconut with your fingers. &nbsp;Combine wet ingredients well, then add to dry. &nbsp;Place all in two 9x13 pans. &nbsp;Cook at 350 for 30 minutes, stirring every 15 minutes. &nbsp;Turn off oven and let it sit in the oven till it is cool. &nbsp;Stir occasionally. &nbsp;Store in sealed container.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cheesy Potato Egg Scramble</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T11">From</span> <span class="T9">Quick Cooking, N/D 2001</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cubed potatoes&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 can&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cheddar cheese soup, undiluted</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">15 pcs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bacon, cooked&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 12 eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lightly beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; margarine&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onion, sliced thin</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In a large skillet, cook potatoes until browned and tender in centers. &nbsp;Sprinkle with salt &amp; pepper and garlic powder. &nbsp;Transfer to greased 2 ½ qt baking dish. Top with soup. Sprinkle half of cooked bacon over soup.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Cook scrambled eggs in butter until nearly set. &nbsp;Spoon over bacon. &nbsp;Sprinkle with grated cheese, remaining bacon (crumbled), and green onion. &nbsp;Bake, uncovered, at 350 for 20-25 minutes or until cheese is melted. &nbsp;Serve with salsa and tortillas for instant breakfast tacos!&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Bacon-Spinach Quiche</span></p>
  <p class="P73">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 9" unbaked pie shells&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl &nbsp;butter, softened</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">2-10oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pkgs frozen chopped spinach, thawed</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">8 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bacon, cooked &amp; crumbled</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whipping cream, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 8 &nbsp;eggs, beaten, divided</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese, divided&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 &nbsp; tsp salt divided</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">2 pinches &nbsp;nutmeg</span></p>
  <p class="P75">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Rub softened butter on the inside surface of pie shell. &nbsp;Drain spinach; squeeze out as much liquid as you can. &nbsp;Place spinach in pie shell and top with crumble bacon. &nbsp;Whisk together half of cream, eggs, cheese, salt, and nutmeg. &nbsp;Pour mixture into pie shell. Repeat for next pie. &nbsp;Bake quiche at 425 for 10 minutes, then reduce heat to 325 for an additional 40 minutes or until quiches are set. &nbsp;Makes 2.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Overnight Oven-Baked French Toast</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; loaf bread&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter, softened</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; maple syrup</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Slice bread, butter each slice on one side, and arrange on baking pan (butter side up). &nbsp;Whisk together remaining ingredients and pour over bread. &nbsp;Press slices down, cover pan and chill 8 hours. &nbsp;Bake, uncovered, at 350 for 45 minutes or until golden.</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Hashbrown Pies</span></p>
  <p class="P76">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">10&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; large eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; real bacon bits&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated raw potatoes</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; green onions, thinly sliced&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hot pepper sauce</span></p>
  <p class="P74"><span class="T30">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P75">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Grease 2 9-inch pie pans. &nbsp;In each of TWO mixing bowls, combine half of all ingredients above except cheese and bacon. &nbsp;Add in 1 c of cheese and 1/3 c of bacon bits into each bowl. &nbsp;Pour each bowlful into a pie pan. &nbsp;Bake 30 minutes or until center is set. &nbsp;Sprinkle remaining bacon and cheese over top of pie. &nbsp;Continue baking 3-5 minutes or until cheese is melted. &nbsp;Serve with salsa. &nbsp;Good reheated. &nbsp;Makes 2 pies.</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Gildner Granola</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Linda Gildner</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">7 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oats&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 jar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; wheat germ</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sweetened, shredded coconut</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped pecans&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; boiling water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; honey</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sunflower seeds, optional&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sliced almonds, optional</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Mix all dry ingredients in LARGE bowl. &nbsp;Mix oil, water and honey together well and pour over dry ingredients. &nbsp;Mix thoroughly. &nbsp;Place mixture into 2 13x9 pans and bake for 15 minutes. &nbsp;Remove from oven, stir, and bake for 15 more minutes. &nbsp;Remove, stir, turn off oven, and return to oven for 15 minutes. &nbsp;Continue to remove, stir and return to oven until granola is dry and crunchy. &nbsp;If it is very humid, turn oven back on to 200 while granola is removed from oven. &nbsp;When up to temp, continue baking, stirring, baking, stirring until dry. &nbsp;Store in cereal container when cooled.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Egg and Sausage Breakfast Casserole</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 lbs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; breakfast sausage&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 loaf &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bread</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¾ lb&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sharp cheddar cheese, grated</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Brown sausage and drain. &nbsp;Place on bottom of greased 13x9 dish. Place bread on top of sausage and put cheese on top of bread.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix with beater in large bowl:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry mustard (break up lumps)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pepper</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Worcestershire sauce&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; half and half</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Pour liquid mixture over ingredients in casserole, cover and refrigerate overnight. &nbsp;Bake for 45-50 minutes in 325 to 350 degree oven. &nbsp;Cut into squares, serve hot.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P29">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Homemade Yogurt</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 gal&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whole milk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 16 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; plain yogurt with live cultures - not nonfat</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Heat milk on stove to 185-195 degrees. &nbsp;DO NOT BOIL. &nbsp;Place in sink of cool water to cool down. &nbsp;Cool milk to 122-130 degrees. &nbsp;Stir in yogurt with whisk until no yogurt clumps appear. &nbsp;Pour into 5 sterile half-gallon jars, seal and place these into roasting oven. &nbsp;Pour warm water around jars until near the top of the roasting oven pan. Place roasting oven lid over jars. &nbsp; Set temp to 125 degrees, insert probe thermometer into center of water bath and maintain temperature of water at 122 to 130 degrees. &nbsp;Yogurt should be set in 3 to 4 hours. &nbsp;The longer it cultures, the more tangy it will be. &nbsp;Refrigerate. &nbsp;Lasts for several weeks in fridge.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Buttermilk Pancakes</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; buttermilk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">9 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla extract</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large bowl, mix &nbsp;together dry ingredients. &nbsp;In separate bowl, combine wet ingredients. &nbsp;Add wet mixture to dry ingredients. &nbsp;Stir until just moistened. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat lightly greased griddle to 325. &nbsp;Drop by scant ¼ cupfuls onto griddle. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P66"><span class="T1">Plain Bagels</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; high-gluten flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; barley malt syrup&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry yeast</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lukewarm water + 12 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornmeal, for dusting baking sheet</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">6 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; wheat gluten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Mix flour, salt, and malt in bowl of standing mixer (you'll use the dough hook). &nbsp;Add yeast and water; mix at lowest speed until dough looks scrappy, like shreds just beginning to come together, about 4 minutes. &nbsp;Increase to speed 2; continue mixing until dough is stiff and smooth - about 8-10 minutes.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Turn dough onto work surface; divide into 8 portions, about 4 oz each. Roll pieces into smooth balls and &nbsp;cover with towel to rest for 5 minutes.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Form balls into donut rings, place on cornmeal-dusted baking sheet, cover tightly with plastic wrap, and refrigerate overnight.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">About 20 minutes before baking, remove dough rings from refrigerator. Adjust over rack to center position and preheat oven to 450. &nbsp;Fill large pot with 3-inches of water; bring to a rapid boil. &nbsp; Working 4 at a time, drop dough rings into boiling water, stirring and submerging loops with slotted spoon until very slightly puffed, 30-35 seconds. &nbsp;Remove rings from water; transfer to wire rack, bottom side down, to drain.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Transfer boiled rings, rough side down, to parchment paper-lined baking sheet. &nbsp;Bake until deep golden brown and crisp, about 14 minutes. Use tongs to transfer to wire rack to cool. &nbsp;Makes 8 bagels - doubling recipe is not recommended, just make several batches.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T1">Soft Pretzels</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; warm water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 1/8 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry active yeast&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; brown sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 1/8 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bread flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; watrm water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coarse salt, to taste&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; melted butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Sprinkle yeast on lukewarm water in mixing bowl; stir to dissolve. &nbsp;Add sugar, salt and stir; add flour and knead dough until smooth and elastic. &nbsp;Let rise at tleast 2-3 hours.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">While dough is rising, prepare a baking soda water bath with 2 cups warm water and 2 tbl baking soda. &nbsp;Be certain to sir often. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">After dough has risen, pinch off bits of dough and roll into a long rope (about ½ inch or less thick) and shape. &nbsp;Dip pretzel insoda solution and place on parchment paper lined baking sheet. Allow pretzels to rise again. &nbsp;Bake in 500 oven for about 7 minutes or until golden. &nbsp;Brush with butter and sprinkle with coarse salt. &nbsp;Or, dip in melted butter and then in a cinnamon/sugar mixture.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P41">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Donna's Beer Muffins</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Linda Gildner</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 5 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">12 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bottle DARK beer&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Prepare pan for 12 muffins. &nbsp;Measure dry ingredients into bowl &amp; pour beer over, stirring to blend. &nbsp;Spoon into pans. &nbsp;Sprinkle cheese over tops before baking. &nbsp;Bake for 20 minutes. &nbsp;Serve hot.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">NOTE: &nbsp;Don't use with Budweiser beer - it doesn't taste good. &nbsp;The darker beers work much better.</span></p>
