  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cornbread for a Crowd</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T31">From Taste of Home F/M 99, pg 54</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornmeal&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 4&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; buttermilk&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vegetable oil</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 425. Grease a 13x9 AND a 9x9 pan with bacon drippings. &nbsp;Preheat the pans in hot oven for a few minutes. &nbsp; In large bowl, combine dry ingredients. &nbsp;Mix well. Combine eggs, buttermilk and oil in medium bowl; stir into dry ingredients just until moistened. &nbsp;Pour into preheated, greased pans and bake at 425 for 20-25 minutes. &nbsp;Serve warm.</span></p>

  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Red Lobster Biscuits</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Linda Gildner</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Bisquick baking mix&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; milk</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; grated cheddar cheese&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter or margarine, melted</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; garlic powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; parsley flakes</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 400. &nbsp;In mixing bowl, combine baking mix, milk and cheese until soft dough forms; beat vigorously for 30 seconds. &nbsp;Drop dough by spoonfuls onto greased baking sheet. &nbsp;Bake at 400 for 10-12 minutes or until lightly browned. &nbsp;In a small bowl, combine butter, garlic powder and parsley; brush over hot biscuits. &nbsp;Serve warm. &nbsp;Makes 12.</span></p>

  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Zucchini Bread</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Southern Living</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; nutmeg</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; veg. oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs, beaten&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shredded zucchini&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped pecans</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine flour, baking powder, baking soda, salt, cinnamon and nutmeg in large bowl. Combine sugar, oil, eggs, and vanilla in another bowl, stirring well. Add to dry ingredients, sturring until just moistened. Stir in zucchini and nuts.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Spoon batter into two lightly greased 8.5x4.5-inch loafpans. Bake at 350 for 50 minutes or until wooden pick inserted in center comes out clean. Cool in pans on wire racks 10 minutes; remove from pans, and cool completely on wire racks.</span></p>

  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Herb Bread</span></p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T12">from Maggie Saenz</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P2"><span style="position:absolute;left:4.445cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:0.905cm;">3 ¼ c</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-0.0949999999999998cm;">hot water</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-1.095cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:-2.095cm;">½ c</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-3.095cm;">whole milk</span></p>
  <p class="P2"><span style="position:absolute;left:4.445cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:0.905cm;">6 tbl</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-0.0949999999999998cm;">dry milk powder</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-1.095cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:-2.095cm;">6 tbl</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-3.095cm;">sugar (or 1/3 cup honey)</span></p>
  <p class="P2"><span style="position:absolute;left:4.445cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:0.905cm;">1 ½ tbl</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-0.0949999999999998cm;">sea salt</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-1.095cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:-2.095cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:-3.095cm;">6 tbl</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-4.095cm;">soft butter</span></p>
  <p class="P2"><span style="position:absolute;left:4.445cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:0.905cm;">¼ c</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-0.0949999999999998cm;">yeast</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-1.095cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:-2.095cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:-3.095cm;">3 c</span><span style="position:absolute;left:-4.095cm;">flour</span></p>
  <p class="P2"><span style="position:absolute;left:4.445cm;"></span><span style="position:absolute;left:0.905cm;">assorted fresh herbs, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Mix until well blended. &nbsp;Let stand for at least 15 minutes, no more than 25. &nbsp;Add more flour until the sides clean. &nbsp;Knead for 7 minutes on speed #2. &nbsp;Form loaves on an oiled counter. Put in greased pans and let rise 30-50 minutes or until high. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 30 minutes or until brown.</p>
  <p class="P10">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P51">Currently, I use 3 tbl of each of these fresh herbs. (I only use 2 tbl if dried.)</p>
  <p class="Standard">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10">Marjoram, thyme, tarragon, rosemary, sage, oregano, basil, chives<span class="T6">.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Corn Muffins</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cornmeal</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry milk powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 ½ oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; can creamed corn&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; unsweetened applesauce</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P59"><span class="T18">Combine flour, cornmeal, dry milk, sugar, baking powder and salt. &nbsp;In another bowl, combine remaining ingredients; mix well. &nbsp;Stir in dry ingredients just until moistened. &nbsp;Fill ,muffin cups two-thirds full. &nbsp;Bake at 350 for 20-25 minutes. Or until muffins test done. &nbsp;Makes 22 muffins.</span></p>
  <p class="P36"><span class="T1">Focaccia Bread</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Dough:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; yeast&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; warm water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">3 ¾ c &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Toppings:</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">oregano, basil, onion powder, garlic powder, pepper, grated Parmesan</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">To make dough, sprinkle yeast over warm water and let stand 5 minutes. &nbsp;Stir in salt, oil, and 2 ½ c flour. &nbsp;Beat until smooth and elastic. &nbsp;Stir in 1 1/3 c more flour. &nbsp;Knead for 10 minutes, adding flour as needed. &nbsp;Place dough in oiled bowl, turn to oil top. &nbsp;Cover and let rise until doubled. &nbsp;Punch dough down. &nbsp;Coat cookie sheet generously with olive oil. &nbsp;Press dough into cooking sheet, pressing and stretching to cover entire sheet. &nbsp;Let rise until double.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Drizzle olive oil over top of dough. &nbsp;Press fingers gently into dough to make dimples. &nbsp;Sprinkle entire surface generously with herbs and cheese. &nbsp;Bake at 400 for 15 minutes. &nbsp;Top generously with grated mozzarella cheese and make 10 minutes more or until cheese is melted.</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Cranberry Nut Bread</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; egg, beaten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; butter</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; honey&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; walnuts, chopped</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cranberries, halved&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; orange juice</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Mix dry ingredients together. &nbsp;Cut in butter until coarse texture. Combine liquid ingredients in another bowl. &nbsp;Pour liquids into dry ingredients all at once and stir only enough to blend everything well. &nbsp;Add nuts &amp; cranberries. &nbsp;Pour into well greased loaf pan and bake 1 hour. &nbsp; We like it with more cranberries, but you have to bake it a little longer.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P54">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Self-Rising Flour</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking powder</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine all very well - sift or use whisk.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Daddy's Cream Biscuits</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 parts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; self-rising flour (he always uses White Lily brand)</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 part&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; whipping cream</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 450. &nbsp;Mix only until moistened. &nbsp;Roll out to ½" thickness, cut into 2" circles, place on cookie sheet 1" apart and bake until lightly browned. &nbsp;Handle dough as little as necessary to keep them flaky. &nbsp;Keep as cold as possible until they hit the oven to ensure they rise the highest.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Sour Cream Banana Bread</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; cinnamon</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; stick butter&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 3&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bananas, very ripe (1c)</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; chopped pecans or walnuts&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sour cream</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 350. &nbsp;Spray 12-inch loaf pan with Pam. &nbsp;Then combine ¼ c sugar and cinnamon. &nbsp;Sprinkle bottom &amp; sides of loaf pan with cinnamon sugar. Cream butter and 1 c &nbsp;sugar. &nbsp;Add eggs and vanilla. Add the dry ingredients; mix. &nbsp;Add the bananas, nuts, and sour cream. &nbsp;Pour batter into prepared pan. &nbsp;Sprinkle top of batter heavily with remaining cinnamon sugar. &nbsp;Bake for 1 hour.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">[Note: &nbsp;3 batches made at once, fills Bosch mixer and makes 4 10-inch loaves. &nbsp;Bake them together for 45-50 minutes.]</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title">Blueberry Banana Bread</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T9">From Taste of Home, J/J 2003</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; all-purpose flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tsp &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; baking soda</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ½ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; shortening</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; eggs</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vanilla&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 med&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; bananas, mashed</span></p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fresh or frozen blueberries</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">In a bowl, combine flour, baking soda, and salt. &nbsp;In a large mixing bowl, cream shortening and sugar. &nbsp;Add eggs and vanilla; mix well. &nbsp;Beat in bananas. &nbsp;Gradually add the dry ingredients, beating just until combined. &nbsp;Fold in blueberries.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Pour into 3 5 ¾ inch x 3 inch x 2 inch mini loaf pans. &nbsp;Bake @ 350 for 30-35 minutes or until a toothpick inserted near center comes out clean. &nbsp;Cool for 10 minutes before removing from pans to wire racks. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P33"><span class="T6">Can also make 2 dozen muffins; reduce cooking time to 20-25 minutes and check centers.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P66"><span class="T1">Whole Wheat Pita Pockets</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ¼ c &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; warm water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; salt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 2 tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sugar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 ¾ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; soft whole wheat flour&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 1/3 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; wheat gluten</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 ½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; dry yeast&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">In large bowl, combine water, oil, salt and sugar. &nbsp;Add the gluten and 1 cup of the flour, along with the yeast, and stir to mix. &nbsp;Add remaining flour and knead to amek a soft dough. &nbsp;Add additional flour if necessary.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Put dough into a bowl, lightly oil the top and cover. Set in a warm place to rise until almost double (about an hour). Punch down dough and turn onto a lightly floured surface. &nbsp;Using a sharp knife, cut dough into 8 equal pieces. &nbsp;Form each piece into a ball. On a lightly floured surface, roll each ball into a 6-7 inch circle. &nbsp;Do not let it get too thin!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">As you roll the rounds, set them aside on a lightly floured countertop and cover loosely with a towel. Let rise for about 30 minutes, until slightly puffy. &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Preheat oven to 500 degrees. Place 2 rounds, side-by-side, onto a wire rack (with the dampest side up). &nbsp;Place rack in the middle of the iven. &nbsp;Bake for 4-5 minutes, until puffy and just slightly browned. &nbsp;Remove immediately and wrap/layer in a damp towel. &nbsp;Continue to bake the other rounds. &nbsp;Makes 8 pita pocket rounds.</span></p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P32">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P70"><span class="T1">Window Washing Solution</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">½ tsp&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; liquid detergent</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">2 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Combine well in bucket. &nbsp;Use on windows to cut grime. &nbsp;Squeegee off glass before it dries.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Liquid Soap</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">8 oz &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; EXACTLY of homemade soap</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">4 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; water</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">**2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; sweet orange essential oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ** these are optional</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">**2 tbl&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lemon essential oil</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Grate soap into small shreds (not the larger size). &nbsp;Bring water to rolling boil. &nbsp;Reduce heat to medium-low. &nbsp;While whisking, add small amounts of grated soap at a time. &nbsp;Let each addition melt into water before adding more. &nbsp;Watch out that pot doesn't foam over! &nbsp;Continue to whisk until all soap has been incorporated. &nbsp;Remove from heat and let cool.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Add OPTIONAL essential oils and mix. &nbsp;Pour through sieve into 1 quart and 1 pint size jars. &nbsp;Let set overnight to thicken. &nbsp;Shake before pouring into dispenser.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Linen Spray</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 c&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; distilled water&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; vodka</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">15 drops&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lavender essential oil</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Put all ingredients into spray bottle and mix. &nbsp;Spray as needed on linens when pressing or making beds.</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Fly Spray</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">¼ oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; citronella essential oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 qt&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; apple cider vinegar</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Put all ingredients into spray bottle and mix. &nbsp;Spray as needed on cows - avoid their eyes!</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="Title"><span class="T1">Moisturizer</span></p>
  <p class="P55">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">1 oz&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; extra virgin olive oil&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 10 drops vitamin E oil</span></p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">10 drops&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; lavender essential oil</span></p>
  <p class="P3">&nbsp;</p>
  <p class="P10"><span class="T6">Put all ingredients into small bottle with dropper top. &nbsp;Put 3-4 drops onto palm and blot gently onto face and neck.</span></p>
